5) What is the process by which God gives us blessings?
Everyone living on this earth, without exception, wishes to receive God's blessings. They wish to be blessed centered around their individual selves. And those who have received God's blessings hope that those blessings will extend to their neighbors or nations. So tonight, I would like to speak on the topic of what the process is by which God gives us blessings. 
The first condition for being able to receive blessings
People use the word blessing easily. However, they do not know how much suffering and pain are behind this blessing, nor do they understand how difficult the process is to reach that point. 
The one who gives us blessings is God. And the ones who receive those blessings are us humans, that is, you. However, in a fallen world, unless humans establish suitable conditions to receive blessings, God cannot bless them. 
We can find a good example of this through the time of Noah. Noah was commanded to endure severe hardships for 120 years before receiving blessings. The period he worked to establish that condition was not 12 months or 12 years, but 120 years. Moreover, the command he received was to build an ark on a mountaintop, not by the sea. When Noah received such a command from God, everyone was skeptical. They thought it was a kind of madness. The people at that time could not even dream of such a thing, so they lived as usual, eating, drinking, and indulging in pleasures while forgetting God. However, for Noah, God's command was absolute. No one truly understood Noah's heart. Only he knew. His wife could not understand, nor could his children understand Noah's situation. What could his relatives have said? It is easy to imagine. 
What God demanded of Noah was to completely abandon his relationship with all of humanity. In order to fulfill this command from God, Noah had to cut off all ties. He could not love his wife or children more than God's command. Noah could choose nothing other than God's command, which was absolute and unshakeable like a rock. How do you think the people of that time treated Noah, who was in such a position? You can easily imagine that. 
In fact, at that time, his wife should have followed her husband. Although it is not recorded in the Bible, it is said that his entire family abandoned Noah, so he was left alone to build the ark. Noah's family rejected his plan. They opposed his will. If he could have gained even a little cooperation from those around him, he could have easily endured the persecution coming from the outside. However, in that position, Noah, who became a grandfather after passing 10, 20, 30...120 years, was known to the world as a madman. 
At that time, only one person, Noah, followed God. All the others gradually drifted further away from God as the days went by. Therefore, from God's perspective at that time, He had no choice but to choose only Noah. God could only rely on Noah's loyalty. There was no other foundation to be found on earth. 
God needed a foundation above all else. The foundation that God needed was severely persecuted in the world. The world repeatedly rebelled against that foundation and God. The condition of that foundation was established by Noah. Therefore, God was able to judge the world based on that foundation. This is just one example. 
Before God blesses any individual, family, tribe, nation, or world that is to take on the mission and responsibility of heaven, He first assures that they can endure any suffering. Therefore, those who take on the mission of heaven must fight, and they must win that fight. This is the first condition required before receiving blessings that you must understand. 
The peaks of trials and hardships
Let’s look at Abraham again. God commanded Abraham to leave his beloved hometown of Ur of the Chaldeans. Abraham had no other way but to obey God's command. He had to go to a foreign land he had never been to before. Yet he believed only in God. Because Abraham was loyal to God in this way, God was able to place him at the center of providence. 
God can only choose an individual who is not subject to Satan's accusations. Therefore, the individual who is chosen must be one who is free from Satan's accusations. This is the first condition that God requires of the individual who is to be central. You must understand that this principle also applies to today's providence. 
The same was true for Jacob. In order for Jacob to receive the blessings promised by God, he had to go to Haran, the symbolic land of Satan. He had to establish the condition of sacrifice. He had to endure unbearable hardships for 21 years. Only then did he receive the name Israel, which signifies victory, and was able to return to Canaan, the land symbolizing the heavenly world. However, he and his 70 family members had to embark on another journey as sojourners for the sake of suffering in Egypt. This is the trial on a tribal level. 
They suffered for 400 years in Egypt. Only after going through such hardships was God able to advance the greater providence of returning the Israelite nation to the land of Canaan under the leadership of Moses. However, the path of trials and hardships became increasingly treacherous. The Israelite nation had to overcome even harsher trials and hardships to establish their expectations for receiving the Messiah. However, the Israelite nation chosen by God at that time did not understand why they had to walk the path of suffering in the restoration of the heavenly world centered around the Messiah. If the Israelite nation had understood the reasons for their suffering and established national expectations, and welcomed the Messiah in unity, the history of humanity today would have been profoundly different. Unfortunately, the Israelite nation failed to fulfill their mission and crucified Jesus Christ. Thus, we could only move in the direction of fulfilling spiritual, national, and cosmic expectations. Because the Israelite nation failed to fulfill their mission, Christian believers after Jesus had to endure suffering and trials. Therefore, Christianity had to move to the Roman Empire, the land of Satan. Thus, Christianity was able to establish a new expectation for global restoration by courageously enduring suffering amidst the persecution of the Roman Empire along with the spiritual Messiah. 
In fact, Jesus should not have died as a sacrificial offering on Calvary. If that had not happened, the saints who followed him could have entered the Roman Empire within 40 years with the living Jesus. Until today, very few have known about this heavenly providence. If Jesus had not died, He could have achieved victory both spiritually and realistically, obtaining a dual victory. 
At that time, the Roman Empire was known as a global empire. The Roman Empire was the center of the world and symbolized the entire world. If the crowds following Jesus had taken the living Jesus as their center, they could have easily subdued the Roman Empire, and from there, they could have overcome global trials and hardships to completely fulfill the will of global restoration. 
The meaning of the blessings given by God
History, in principle, repeats itself. At the same time, history is preparing for a dramatic day when the purpose of human history will be achieved, the day of the end of the world. In other words, it is moving in a direction to set up the same conditions as at the time of Jesus' first coming. During this time, God does not remain idle. He is moving to create better conditions, atmosphere, and environment to establish a new religious focus. By establishing freedom of the press, freedom of assembly, and freedom of religion, He has prepared everything for a new religion to be born. This is why democracy, as a new political form that can build a free world, has emerged. You must clearly understand this fact. 
Today, the United States stands in the same position as the Roman Empire did 2,000 years ago. The United States, which can be called the Rome of the 20th century, must not be like the Rome of the 1st century that only boasted of its culture. It must also not only strive to dominate other countries. 
God's blessings are absolutely public. Those blessings are not for any individual alone, nor for any family, nation, or world alone. God's blessings are for the entire universe. 
Brothers of America gathered here today, you must understand how much suffering God has endured to grant great blessings on this earth and to prepare this moment. Now, the great ideology must truly take root on this earth.
We must ensure that a great ideology, which recognizes that the entire world is one family, is born from above. 

Let us examine recent world history. After World War II, the global trend has leaned towards the independence of all nations and peoples. The truly authentic and genuine history of humanity was destroyed due to the conflict between the two brothers, Cain and Abel. Cain killed his younger brother Abel. In this era, where we must restore the tragedy of human history, brotherhood must be reestablished from a global perspective. 

The brothers and sisters of the Unification Church, who have embarked on the principle movement, must understand that God has shed countless tears, sweat, and blood to bless us. Therefore, just as God has done for us, we also have the responsibility to do the same. We have already resolved not to spare our tears, sweat, and blood for our comrades. We must share the blessings we have received with all humanity. If the blessings that America enjoys today are not shared with people around the world, and if you cannot shed tears, sweat, and blood for people around the world, then all nations will rebel against you. You must clearly understand that you will also face ruin. Therefore, you must take the lead and become exemplary groups in giving all that you have for the people of the world. 

The respected former President Kennedy established a new pioneering spirit. This pioneering spirit is precisely what symbolizes this era. Furthermore, he founded the Peace Corps, which could lead to the era of heaven and God's providence. 

In serving all humanity, there is now a difference in the method of receiving God's blessings compared to the past. In the past, to receive God's blessings, one had to abandon everything they had and go to a foreign land. However, today, we must not abandon anything. We must take everything we have and share it. This is goodness. 

There is a wonderful principle in giving. It is that you must embody God's love and heart while performing the role of a servant. You must possess God's heart while using the body of a servant. And you must go out to humanity and give all that you have. 

What is the most precious thing you possess? You must be able to give it without any regrets or hesitation. The most precious possessions for you are your tears, sweat, and blood. You must sweat for all things. You must shed your blood for heaven. You must weep for humanity. This is the motto of the principle movement. We must be able to freely share these things. Only then can we become one spiritually and emotionally. 

Furthermore, we must seek the lost true children, true siblings, true families, true nations, and the true world. Restoring these true things is not an easy or simple task. True things are not easily found. Happiness cannot be discovered in what is easily found. 

We have lost the blessings of heaven to the world of Satan. Because the world of Satan belongs to Cain, Abel must restore the world of Satan through Cain. Thus, Jacob had to serve Esau. Jesus also had to restore everything through serving the chosen people. Therefore, you must serve all people. This is the formula for restoration. 

Those who are within the realm of heavenly blessings must help those who are not. You must be able to place others before yourselves. Only then can you occupy the best positions. You must help them and push them forward so that they can reach their destination. 

Let me give you an example. No matter how blessed a country America may be, it cannot achieve the ultimate purpose of the providence of restoration by itself. To achieve that ultimate purpose, it must help all the impoverished people of other countries. We must push forward with the suffering humanity ahead of us. In fact, today, America is approaching that purpose. However, I wish that more of America's budget would be spent on the noble purpose of helping humanity around the world. 

Today, the relationship between America and Vietnam is a good example. It may seem unrelated to you, but in reality, they are intertwined in some way. This is the era we live in today. Therefore, America is helping all regions that are causing problems. You must treat those lands with the same sense of responsibility as you would your own. You must serve all humanity. 

Mission First
Do you wish to be sons and daughters loved by God? God has come to find you through a place of indescribable sacrifice. He has walked the path of giving up everything to find you who can achieve the ultimate purpose. God has sought you while sacrificing the most precious things. In this way, God has given all of Himself infinitely while enduring infinite suffering. 

But what position have you been in? You have been in a position to receive blessings. If so, what kind of determination have you made to endure suffering like God? To become true sons and daughters of God, we must awaken for a new realization. Furthermore, we must be fully prepared for new practices. 

When God's ultimate purpose is achieved and blessings are received, will you be able to give up everything you have without any regrets? Will you be able to abandon your possessions, your children, and your family? Ultimately, will you be able to give up yourself for the sake of the entire world? Can you offer your children, your wife, your husband, and even your own life? No matter what kind of suffering may be in that process, God has walked that path to find you. God did not compromise with anything to walk that path. 

If today, the 180 million American citizens are fully prepared to give their most precious things for the noble and sacred purpose of all humanity, the entire world could be restored overnight. However, the current situation in America is somewhat different from what we hope for. Therefore, you, who have been chosen as pioneers of the principle movement, must carve out an exemplary path for your American brothers and sisters. In fact, the path I have walked until now has been such a path. 

I once abandoned my parents. When I was in prison, my parents came to me and advised me to stop what I was doing. That was like stabbing me with a knife, so I immediately rejected that request. After liberation in 1945, I was living in South Korea with my family. However, upon receiving God's command, I realized that it was not good to live there. So, I had to leave South Korea. I had to go to North Korea, which was occupied by communists, leaving my entire family behind and going alone. 

God always thinks of Himself last. He always thinks of you who live on this earth first. God does not prioritize what is for Himself. He worries, cares for, and loves you who are on this earth while forgetting Himself. I too had to walk the same path as God the Father. What I love most and what is closest to me must be accepted last. No matter what happens, I must go out with mission first. 

I truly had a brother who loved me. He had some spiritual experiences, and among my family, he was the only one who vaguely understood my mission. No one else in my family knew that I had a mission regarding the principle and that I had the intention to raise a new movement that could present the final answer before heaven and earth. However, I loved my family. I loved my mother and my siblings. Nevertheless, I could not tell them the amazing truth about the principle before anyone else. I could not reveal the principle to them before others. This was because the center had to be established before the surroundings could be arranged. Therefore, I had to relate to others, and furthermore, to the world, before standing before God's standard. The people of the world must accept the principle before my family does. The surroundings must be established before the center is determined. 

America must be the stepping stone for world restoration
I have truly served people as I would serve my father and mother. Furthermore, to establish expectations for the restoration of society and the nation, I have treated even strangers in such a way. Under this principle, I could not only be concerned for my own nation. Even amidst the most severe persecution, my prayers and concerns were not for Korea. I did my best to send missionaries to Japan and America. 

When I sent missionaries to Japan, Korea and Japan did not have normal diplomatic relations. Therefore, the missionaries had to cross over to Japan on a small boat without following normal procedures. So, you can imagine how much suffering we endured when we sent a single missionary to America. At that time, sending a missionary to America was something no one could think of. Despite such circumstances, I was determined to send someone to sow the seeds of the principle in America and worked tirelessly day and night. 

The principle of restoration is to come from the outside in. Therefore, for America to receive the glorious blessings from God, the providential will must come from the outside in. We must not start from within America. This is your responsibility. Because of this position, you must embark on a long journey. Your life and death depend on this mission. 

For the restoration of America, for the restoration of the world, and for the restoration of the universe, your family is not the issue. Your pride is not the issue. Great things cannot be achieved without sacrifice. I believe the time has come for America to awaken anew. A new dawn must come to the land of America. 

You must take responsibility for all the states in America. Your activities must expand from this state to other states. Even if your numbers are limited, each of you must fulfill this responsibility. If you in America fail to fulfill this responsibility, do you know what will happen? If that happens, America, in the position of Abel, will suffer through the communist regime in the position of Cain. The entire free world will face calamity. However, if you feel this significant mission and fulfill your responsibilities, you will be able to save democracy and establish freedom. In that case, the communist world will automatically perish. 

The meaning of the principle movement centered on Korea and America
In today's providence of God, Korea is in a position to receive the foundation of America economically. The relationship between Korea and America today is exactly like the relationship between the Jewish kingdom and the Roman Empire 2,000 years ago. Why must the movement of recreation start in a country like Korea? The historical basis lies here. 

You can find similarities between the time when the greatest ideology was revealed in the insignificant nation of Israel 2,000 years ago and today. The reason is that the great ideology must be spread throughout the world. In light of God's providence, America represents the nation of Western civilization. America has achieved this civilization today through learning, research, and analysis. Furthermore, it has built today's culture on this scientific foundation. I call this external civilization. The more knowledge you acquire on such a foundation, the more global victories you will achieve. 

However, external things alone cannot satisfy all the demands of humanity. There must necessarily be internal elements required. The prosperity of internal elements and external culture must unite. As mentioned earlier, the more scientific knowledge you acquire, the more victories you will achieve. However, conversely, the more religious or spiritual knowledge you acquire, the more material possessions you will lose. In other words, efforts in science, which involve analysis and research, make humanity prosperous. However, this is merely external. Conversely, those who are engrossed in internal civilization, namely spirituality or religion, will lose external things. 

Do you know why? The reason is very simple. The spirit is not material. Therefore, a nation that has lost all material possessions must be chosen among the Eastern nations. 

From a historical perspective, today, the East and West are facing a stage where they must unite. At such a time, we must become one. In this way, at the end, a nation that can unify the entire civilization of humanity, that is, a nation that can achieve cosmic completion both spiritually and materially, must emerge. When that happens, the entire world will surely become rich both spiritually and materially. 

Many countries in the East have great expectations for America's external success. At the same time, you in America must also have expectations for internal success. This is what the principle movement signifies. You must understand that we are at a crossroads for unity. As mentioned at the beginning, to receive God's blessings, you must overcome many pains and trials. That is your sacred responsibility. Knowing all of this, you must now be able to give your most precious things to the suffering people of the world. You must be fully prepared to respond to that great calling. 

I will say it again here. You must not only share your most precious things with those within the free world but also extend that range to those within the communist world. The final victory will come when we infinitely give, infinitely love, and infinitely sacrifice for them.
for the sake of the world. However, now we must expand beyond the nation and make sacrifices on a national level. Without a national sacrifice, we cannot achieve a national altar or national offerings. This is the issue we face.

In the past, sacrifices were made by individuals or families, and the Israelite people as a tribe made sacrifices for the sake of the world. But now, we must transcend these boundaries and create a national sacrifice that can serve as an altar for the world. Without this, we cannot fulfill our mission.

The world is in need of a new foundation built on sacrifice. We must establish a national altar that can serve as a beacon of hope and a source of strength for all humanity. This is the path we must take to realize the ideals of God.

We must understand that the sacrifices we make are not just for ourselves or our immediate surroundings, but for the greater good of humanity. Our sacrifices must resonate throughout the world, inspiring others to join us in our mission.

As we move forward, we must remain steadfast in our commitment to this cause. We must be willing to endure hardships and challenges, knowing that our sacrifices will ultimately lead to the realization of a better world.

Let us unite in our efforts to create a national sacrifice that will serve as a foundation for the world. Together, we can overcome the obstacles in our path and achieve the victory that God desires for us.
Oh, it has come out. However, the problem is the offering as one nation. There is no such country today. This is God's lament, and at the same time, it is our lament. When the teacher travels to various countries, even if he stays in that country for just two days, he often feels the impulse to give everything he has. 

When the heart connects, everyone becomes a child of God. Human value is not determined by cultural backgrounds, historical environments, or the position of the times. Nothing can determine human value. Human value is determined only when one knows heaven, knows the earth, and knows the purpose of heaven, the purpose of the earth, and the purpose of humanity. Therefore, you must follow where God intends to go or where the teacher desires to go. God and the teacher do not engage with you to use you. It is not for individual purposes but for the whole, and it is for the future beyond this world.

Today, this era is miserable. That is why the Japanese family must unite by holding hands together with the sacred hearts of youth. Although your numbers may be small, the purpose you hold transcends the strength of the entire Japanese nation, so no external force can divide you. The more you collide, the more united you must become because of that strength. So, what should you unite for? To establish a national altar and become a nation that can offer that national offering to the world, God desires you to unite for this purpose. That is why God has fought for the purpose of His providence for the past 6,000 years. Therefore, you must have the strength and resolution to endure all sacrifices and hardships, even if you find yourselves in the most miserable positions, to overcome and rise above them.

Now, in 1967, it will be 21 years since the teacher embarked on this path of purpose. As I think about traveling around the world this time, I feel how wonderful it would be if the teacher were just a little younger, perhaps around 30 years old... I have felt such things. Because there is still so much to do.

How should we walk the path of restoration? Now the teacher is over 40 years old. From the perspective of the restoration path, the time to fulfill the purpose of restoration is approaching. Now you are entering a stage where you must fight for a decisive victory. Therefore, if you dedicate a nation to God, it will become an offering for the entire world, and the future world will entrust everything to this nation. This is an ironclad principle. That is why when the teacher goes to Korea, he cannot help but command the weary Korean family. Thus, it often pains my heart, making it truly difficult to endure. How many years can we endure? Three years, seven years, 21 years, 40 years... It is a problem.

The path to becoming a heavenly offering. Now you should not think of any success or purpose centered around yourselves. Demanding success for Japan is for the sake of seeking success for the entire world. If you, even just as you are now, unite to fulfill the mission of restoring Japan, it won't even take 20 years. To fulfill that mission, you will need offerings without rest. An offering must not have its own subjectivity. Therefore, when dealing with the whole, you must have a subjectivity centered on God and determine your position of existence. This is the mission of the offering. To be an offering, one must never assert their own subjectivity.

Today, the fallen world is fighting to determine their own positions of existence. However, such things will inevitably be swept away by the rough waves of history. Therefore, if you move forward from a standard that does not center on yourselves but on the whole, Japan will soon be restored. The teacher knows this country called Japan well. If you think about these things and establish your purpose on a national standard, it will result in saving this world. This is the path that God desires and the path that the teacher desires. Moreover, this is a path that you must take, and it is a path that our Unificationists must take. If you leave this path and die, it is a path you must take even after death. This path is so important that the teacher wants to do global work centered around Tokyo. He wants to move the world once.

To do that, you must become the main characters who can take responsibility for the most difficult places in Tokyo. You must also be able to stand in the most challenging positions of the Japanese Unification Church and take on difficult tasks. Otherwise, Japan will find itself in the most difficult national position. To achieve our goals, we must continue to advance endlessly for ten years, a hundred years. If we cannot achieve it in our generation, we must achieve it through the descendants of the second and third generations. When the global wave sweeps through, the number of people who jump into it will determine the national victory.

Our Unification Church members are engaged in an invisible global movement. At some point, it will manifest on this earth and become a problem. That time will surely come. When that time comes, if Japan is first, Japan will become the center of the world. When it becomes the center, it will be pulled from all directions. When that happens, wisdom will be needed to gather that pulling force. The problem lies in that.

When the teacher prays, he often prays like this. "Is this what the spirits require? Wasn't this the wish of your ancestors? Don't you want to fulfill that purpose? If so, gather together. Let's decide victory and defeat. If you defeat me, I will grant it!" He may also step on and kick to create a foundation for 3.2 billion people. However, good things are all pulled together. Bad things all push back.

Such a time will surely come. If it does not come, I will make it come! This is the teacher's hobby. To do this, no matter how much it is a prison, the teacher can go as if it were next door.

Sometimes there are moments when one fears death. Why? Because there is no successor. So at times, I hesitate for a moment.

How about you? Can you complete your mission with such determination? You must be able to rise again even if you fall and fall. The teacher needs comrades like that.

Japan once claimed the Greater East Asia Co-Prosperity Sphere. Beyond that, it was a good thing. Because of that, Southeast Asia may have been able to shine even more. However, if you go to the dark alleys of one country in Southeast Asia and ask, "What do you think of Japan? How do you view it in the East?" most will not give a good answer. If at that time Japan had truly paid its national power and sacrifice for them, today's Japan would have become a country to be proud of in the world. So what should Japan do? It must sow goodness.

The fruits of goodness. Goodness must be sown well to grow well. If goodness is not sown well, it cannot sprout. Also, if goodness is not nurtured well, it cannot bear fruit. It will not bear fruit if left carelessly. If goodness is treated carelessly and lost, it will receive heavenly judgment. This is a heavenly principle and an ironclad principle. Therefore, when we sow goodness, we must sow it well. We must mobilize the Japanese people to sow it throughout the world. It must be sown with the utmost sacrifice and the utmost effort. If we sow with sincerity like this, our historical ancestors will bow their heads and feel grateful to us.

If someone from another ethnicity comes to Japan and sincerely sows the seeds of goodness, your ancestors will shed tears. They will shed true tears of gratitude. However, the people on this earth do not know this. We are those who sow the seeds of goodness. If we sow with a sincere heart and dedication, we will never fail. Moreover, no one can arbitrarily occupy this. Only the true sons and daughters of heaven can occupy this. Therefore, you must recognize this fact and sacrifice with a new determination and enthusiasm for the future of Japan, and furthermore, you must sow the seeds of goodness throughout the world with the utmost sincerity. 

This is the wish and purpose that God has for you. Moreover, this path is the path that we humans must ultimately take. If you move Japan with this spirit, the world will naturally move as well.

To do this, it is not necessary to have many countries. If even one country unites, everything can be resolved. If such a movement arises in Japan, the teacher will gather all the people of the world to this Japan. People from Africa, America, regardless of color, will be gathered here for the sake of this country. And whenever I go anywhere, I will not go alone but will always take the Japanese people with me. When that happens, Japan will become a global nation. This is something that can realistically be realized.

Twenty-three years ago, when the teacher was studying in Tokyo, he traveled a lot around Tokyo. There was no place he did not visit. This was because he had future plans.

In a few years, the youth of Japan will surely rise. While thinking about this. 

The teacher wants to place you at the forefront and have you travel to various places. However, there is no time for that now. The Japan-Korea issue has become complicated. It has become a national issue. It has become a global issue. In the midst of this, the teacher knows well what will happen to religion.

The path we must take. The future issue for you is that you must unite. Regardless of color, everyone must unite. When these colors are combined and rotated, it produces a white color like sunlight. If various colors are mixed, it appears black, but when it is rotated, it becomes white. Therefore, when everything becomes a composite and rotates, it radiates light, and that light covers the world.

When there is a reaction, strength emerges. When strength emerges, it acts, and when it acts, it moves. And it radiates light. Therefore, you must unite, whether it is Hokkaido or Kyushu, and go out not with a sense of regional superiority but with a sense of national unity. Ultimately, the problem lies with each individual. We must shed everything. If I can be naked and save the entire 100 million, I must shed everything.

The teacher sincerely wishes for you to contribute to all of Japan and even to all of Asia. Do you have the confidence to do such things? Now is the time to prepare for that. The path of paying sacrifices and sincerely sowing the seeds of goodness is the path that our Unificationists must take, and it is the path that God also desires. I ask you to deeply engrave this in your hearts and not to forget it.

Heavenly Father! I know well the countless miserable positions you have endured until now. Please protect the beloved members in Japan. I sincerely ask that you guide them to become young people who can contribute to the new fields in the future path that Japan must take. Please keep the fellowship of the coming days and guide everyone to align with your will, I earnestly pray in the name of True Parents. Amen.

Where are we going? People are wonderful because they can feel about themselves. The standards they set for themselves are not conquered by anyone. Become the owner of the heart. During street evangelism, beloved brothers of Japan will shout, "Come to the Unification Church!" When you come, what will you do? You will awaken. And when you recognize that you have awakened from your sleep, you will be told to go! You can go far away, without a destination. The teacher truly commands this.

Jesus, who stands before Heaven
Matthew 26:36-46
<Prayer> May this holy day be in accordance with your will, and may today's gathering be a holy assembly. When I stand before the Father with my shortcomings, I have nothing to say about what I have done. There are those who are satisfied with the past and present.

When I think that you desire the true, I realize that I have not prepared anything trustworthy in history. I know I have nothing that can be your hope. 

We are those who cannot even long for, think of, or desire your eternal and unchanging love, which all of creation longs for. However, thinking of the countless good ancestors who sacrificed to establish today, and that you have longed for true children whom you can believe in, hope for, and love, I feel deeply that I have nothing to say from my heart and can only kneel and repent before you. The saints of Japan have gathered through years of tears, blood, and sweat. We are those who have fulfilled that mission to respond to your wishes until now. 

We feel sorrowful that we have not been able to establish people worthy of your heart on this earth, even as we have continued history for over 6,000 years. Therefore, we, who have gathered here, earnestly hope that this time will be one where we reaffirm our will and resolve as children who will fulfill your wishes and solidify our greatest vows. 

May this time today be kept, and may we inherit the highest purpose standard of prayer that Jesus prayed in Gethsemane, becoming true children of God who can achieve the final victory and resolve historical grievances. We are grateful for the time given to gather those who have longed for you in their hearts, and we earnestly hope that you will protect all our family members in the future, and we offer everything before you in your name. Amen. 

<Words> We must acknowledge God, who exists as an absolute being in this universe. If God exists, He must have some purpose. If there is a purpose, there must be hope. It is natural that if we are to inherit that hope to the level of purpose, the greater the purpose, the more difficult it is to feel the heart of love in daily life. 

The Fall of Adam and Eve and God's Sorrow
God created all things with the purpose of love. On the sixth day, as the center of this universe, as the central figure to complete the purpose, as the embodiment of hope, and as the pioneer of a life that aligns with God's will, Adam and Eve, our ancestors, were established as those who must set the standard of heart. 

From the moment God created our ancestors, He could not help but think about when the day of hope, which is my purpose, would come through daily life. Adam and Eve, standing before such God, bore the mission of completing God's purpose. 

Thus, when God looked at Adam, He wanted to believe in Adam. He wanted to have infinite hope for Adam. He wanted to pour out infinite affection. This was God's position. 

As young Adam grew, the standard of hope and affection that God could believe in had to grow together, and this universe had to fulfill God's highest purpose, centered on God's love. God sought to realize a unified world where all creation could feel as He thinks and feels, a world that could not be divided even if it tried to be shared. 

However, unexpectedly, Adam and Eve fell on that day. With the day of the Fall, God lost the trustworthy expectations, the standard of hope, and the embodiment of love. As a result, God's creation purpose remained unfulfilled. As a result of the Fall, humanity, the descendants of Adam and Eve, has continued to drift further away from God over time, moving in the opposite direction of the purpose God desires. They have rebelled against God's hope, against the expectations God could believe in, and have fled from the position where God could love them. 

However, it cannot be left as it is. The motivation for this situation lies with humanity, but the ultimate motivation lies with Satan, who tempted humanity. Therefore, here, God must defeat the enemy Satan and restore the original purpose. 

In this process of restoration, the further humanity moves away from God, the more effort God must exert to bridge that gap. Sacrifices must be made. This is because humanity has not stood in the position to make that effort themselves. Satan has not stood in the position to help with that. Only God has stood in the position to do so. 

Originally, Adam and Eve were to connect with God's heart and, while resonating with God's hope, become subjects who are satisfied in the embrace of God’s joy and express gratitude for everything. However, God's internal heartache at seeing them not walk that path was greater than their own internal misery, which our ancestors did not realize. 

However, God, who cannot abandon the concept of purpose centered on His fundamental principles, must realize it no matter what happens. In other words, He must restore it. We must not forget that there is a path of great righteousness and a path of salvation that God did not foresee. Therefore, God has longed for trustworthy sons and daughters, those who were the hope at the time of creation, and He has never failed to think of each one of them through the historical process, through each era and moment. However, our ancestors could not feel this. Countless people have passed from this earth to the spirit world since Adam and Eve, but they too could not realize God's deep internal heart. For this reason, God has not had even one trustworthy person among humanity throughout 1,600 years of history.

Restoration Providence Centered on Noah
From there, God, who must find one person who would run straight to Him and say, "I will only contribute to God," sought to establish that standard through Noah. If God could not find the standard of agreement where people believe in God as God believes in them, God could not start the providence by overcoming Satan. Because of such concerns, God had to command the path of effort to raise Noah to the standard of believing in God for 120 years. 

Noah had to regard the day of the flood judgment, which would come after 120 years, as a hope and the period until then as a time of faith expectation, and he had to connect his hope and faith expectation with God's affection and faith. This was God's providence. It was not for one year or ten years, but for a long period of 120 years that Noah repeated the same task every day. 

If you think that his family welcomed that, it is a great mistake. It was not about something happening in 12 days or even 12 years. It was 120 years. 

The family members did not know whether they would die or not. During that time, they all began to complain about Noah. What did God want from him, who was rejected by the environment? 

"Believe only in me." 

In the midst of all the swirling events around him, there was not a single person who was fully loyal to God. 

However, even if everyone rebelled and rose up, he had to establish a standard of faith that aligned with him by stepping on or repelling them. Thus, he had to fulfill the purpose of God's judgment along with that faith and hope. Therefore, the connection of affection begins at the standard of approaching God with gratitude in the continuous daily life. For this purpose, God established Noah to build the ark. 

So, when God looked at Noah, He naturally worried that Noah might again stand in a position that would rebel against the trustworthy standards of God, just like Adam and Eve. God knew well that if Noah stood in such a position again, it would become a difficult problem. Watching Noah's daily life of building the ark, God knew well how much more indemnity would be required if Noah retreated. God's heart, filled with such worries, passed each day, a feeling that Noah himself did not know. 

Because the purpose of restoration centered on the family of Adam became unfulfilled, the eight members of Noah's family were needed to restore it. Without this one fact being thorough, the second work could not be initiated. However, the absolute standard that the parents must be centered on and that the three sons must unite was broken due to their ignorance, resulting in God's providence being extended for 400 years. 

Thus, God had to establish Abraham as the center of faith. He had to establish him as the standard of hope. He had to establish him as a responsible person who could fulfill the mission of purpose completion. God had to trace back and follow the path of affection behind him. 

Mistakes Made by the Ancestors of Faith
However, Abraham did not know God's internal heart. Abraham thought that even if God cast away the universe, He believed in him with hope, that he was fulfilling the mission of achieving God's purpose, and that God entrusted everything to him. He did not realize that he had to establish the principles of judgment in every aspect of his actions and that he had to establish the laws of judgment that could judge even enemies. 

Moreover, he did not fully feel that this was a standard he had to carry out through his life. Therefore, when he offered the three sacrificial offerings to God, he did not consider that the condition of not splitting the dove would become a miserable condition of indemnity that must be fulfilled through history. He did not understand that it was the final point where the conditions of the heavenly principles could be established in the heavenly restoration process.

History moves. The times call. The future desires us. All of this must start from God. One must pass through that standard.

Because that day exists, we can gain a living environment to receive God's love. The modern world is occupied by evil. The positions and environments occupied by evil are filled with Satan's side. To send such a precious son, the environment had to be created. There had to be individuals who followed God's desire. There had to be families. Jesus, who was the purpose and hope of all, came as the Messiah. He came among the national rights standing on the foundation where the Israelite nation was trying to decide victory. He had to live a public life. Looking back, he realized that the hopes of countless ancestors in the spirit world were hanging on him. He also knew that he had to become a historical offering through Satan's accusations in the world of Satan. 

What would the heart of Jesus, who stood in such a cosmic mission, have been like? How serious was the internal preparation period before he started his public life with such feelings? This is not recorded in the Bible. Of course, at that time, Jesus could not do anything for the crowds who came to rely on him for daily food. However, he had to resurrect history. One cannot build a living history by inheriting a dead history. Without an environment, one cannot properly establish the standard of existence. Only when there is an environment does the standard of existence arise. This is the situation on earth. 

Therefore, Jesus had to establish the standard of good hope on this earth and relate to the good environment of the nation that God had created until now. That was not an individual relationship but a historical relationship. It was a global relationship. It was a future relationship. Since He originally came as a Savior, it is not true that He came with a fate that could not avoid being crucified to forgive our sins. There is no such God. 

To think that there was no way of salvation without such a method, such a way as an omniscient and omnipotent God, is an insult to God. It does not make sense to say that he was crucified by heavenly fate. Not only that, but God also hoped to create an environment where one could live in accordance with the historical standards of faith, hope, and heart, and sent John the Baptist. 

To inherit history, one had to offer a historical offering to determine victory. Otherwise, He could not give the historical sphere. Why? Because due to repeated failures until now, God could not remove the insults suffered from various conditions by Himself. If that were possible, the restoration of God's purpose, which He has been working on for 6,000 years, would not be a problem. Salvation would not be a problem. However, what is wrong must be corrected according to principle. To correct it, one must leave behind a good part that exceeds the opposite. Otherwise, there will be no way to use it even if it is corrected. 

Therefore, Jesus had the mission to bear all the conditions that ancestors had wronged over the past 4,000 years and to establish a standard of value that could start toward God. If he did not do so, he could not start from the world of new hope of God from the world of Satan. Jesus was in such a position. And in that position, he had to comfort God. 

Such Jesus had no face to show to God, who had hoped for 4,000 years, relying on him as the only hope. Therefore, he had to lead and rebuild the Israelite nation. When he thought about the nation that had been raised as a people or as children rebelling against God, he felt he had no face to show to God. Thus, Jesus walked alone at the foot of the Mount of Olives, praying with a heart of concern. It is recorded in the Bible that he had many such times. He also went to John the Baptist at the Jordan River to resolve his internal struggles. 

Jesus, as God's only begotten son, had to start a life of victory and glory with God's absolute protection from God's love, hope, and absolute faith. 

Then, who was John the Baptist? He was the representative of the Israelite nation, a messenger sent by God to represent the Israelite nation, a central figure who could draw the historical Israelite nation into God's expectation as a living sacrifice before Jesus. John the Baptist was the person sent by God with such a mission. Therefore, it was Jesus' mission to establish John the Baptist with 100 percent faith, 100 percent hope, and 100 percent love, and to offer him to God based on the standard that was in harmony with himself.

The Teacher’s Principle
When your country is at war, the teacher was in Japan, and he would often walk around the back alleys of Shinjuku. Wherever he went, he would ask about the past of women. He would have them bring beer. Then they would keep bringing it. However, he does not drink. He sits next to them and talks. 

Why did he come to such a place? While looking at their faces, he would ask if they had no parents. Is your mother not around? Then they gradually open their hearts and start saying yes. So he continued to study that. Wherever he goes, he takes what is beneficial to him. Even if he goes to a bad place, he digests what he can. The teacher has that principle. He is not someone who wanders around looking for a good environment. 

It does not make sense to say that one must go into a quiet and solemn place or a deep mountain to cultivate oneself. The idea that one can only study in a quiet place does not apply to the teacher. He studies even in factories where millions of horsepower motors or engines are running. He does that well. He prepares while doing various things. Sometimes he enters places where things break, and sometimes he goes to places where he is hit…. 

When a great gang bullies the weak, he takes them all on alone. He fights. Alone, just himself. That is for the public good. When he meets, he is alone. The feeling at the moment of being hit is a necessary issue in life philosophy. 

If there is such a person, he will confront and grab hold of that situation and tell his past. If he does not talk about his own affairs, the other party will not treat him sincerely. If he does not speak of his own factual matters, the other party will not treat him sincerely either. It is true that the listener will not become sincere. That is why he speaks of his own matters. 

The teacher often lived a life that was pitiful and like that of a beggar. He felt desperately that a single newspaper in the cold was worth more than a silk blanket. One cannot know that unless they experience it. By speaking of facts, he connects with the truth. That is necessary. 

Let us train our Unification Youth like that. Let us raise cool humans, young people. Wherever you go, kneel down, talk to each other, and communicate. If one does not know that, that is how it is. If one cannot become a person with flavor, they cannot be flavorful….

When the teacher came to Japan, he was young, just like you, but he had great interest in such places and even worked in factories. For example, he often worked in coal transportation at the Kawasaki shipyard. “Let’s do it!” and he would take his friends along. When working, he competed with the company workers. He would ask, “How many hours will you take to do this? We must not lose to them.” He would encourage them strongly and start. If he said they would do it in 4 hours, they would finish it in 3 hours. Then he would come back and sleep for about 3 days. Young people need that kind of thing.

Going up and coming down again

The Fundamental of the Universe and the Value of Humanity  
Cultural lecture? To put it in old terms, it is a time for self-cultivation. What will the teacher talk about?  
Q: Please tell us about the size of the universe.  
If one does not expand their heart, they will not understand. (Laughter)  
Q: How did you find the principle of creation?  
That is not something to ask. When I receive such questions, I become somewhat weak. More importantly, it is about how one acknowledged the existence of God. The principle of creation began with the existence of God. Does God exist or not? Thinking about such things makes one serious. Reflecting on the memories of when I used to wonder if God existed makes me serious.  
To think about God, one must first think about oneself. Where did I come from? I came from my mother. Then where did my mother come from? From my mother's mother... How far back should we trace? How did humanity come to be? Was it truly created by God? There are countless races living, so which lineage do I belong to? What kind of relationship do I have with other people? These are all issues that must be experienced. This applies to everything from one to ten.

The relationship between people and God, what is it centered around, and what is the key point? That is the question.

What is God's desire? Just like our lives, God must also have circumstances. What are God's circumstances? What is the heart of the world that God delights in centered around? What is God's purpose? All of these become questions. If we sum up all these issues of hope and heart, it becomes humanity.  
Then, what connects the relationship between people and God? One cannot know without passing through the standard of heart. Go deep and pray. Ask while praying. What is the fundamental of the universe? It is the parent-child relationship. The first standard is that humanity and God are in a parent-child relationship. The fundamental of the universe is the parent-child relationship centered on heavenly heart and heavenly lineage.  
Then, are the parents who gave birth to you your true parents? How can one enter that realm of heart that cannot be denied by any reasoning? That question can only be known through heart.  
When one cries out, "Heavenly Father!" all things in the universe gather there. The term "Father" is a definition of the whole. It feels like the central word of all representations. One must enter that position. No matter what thoughts arise in one's heart, they cannot deny that God is their parent. And God also says about themselves, "Yes." There, an undoubtable parent-child relationship is established.  
Therefore, the fundamental of the universe is parent-child. All things are a garden for the children. If one knows God for sure, the principle of creation will naturally emerge. My mind and body are in such a relationship. By establishing a standard of relative value centered on God, one can maintain the expectation of a son-in-law.  
To maintain that permanently, one must engage in reciprocal actions. By doing so, if one knows God for sure, they will naturally come to realize the principle of creation.  
You are learning the principle, and you must understand that the principle you hear only in words was obtained after the teacher fought through countless footprints. Speaking of the Adam family, unless one enters a stage beyond the fall of the sun centered on the teacher, they cannot correct the mistakes made by the sun. And if we do not comfort God’s sorrow caused by the fall of Adam, God cannot give us the standard of true joy.  
Therefore, one must resolve the standard of indemnity with heart. In the historical realm of heart, one must enter deeply into God's inner circle to comfort God and create a standard where God can relate to us. The teacher is the pioneer and the seer of that path. Until now, the teacher has done that work alone. That is magnificent. Carrying the weight of thousands of years of history, untangling all the wrong connections, and creating a single path is a global contribution. It counts as the greatest success in human history. Establishing the standard of victory from the spirit world and connecting it to the earthly realm.  
Q: When did you start thinking about God?  
Since I was young. The teacher was different from childhood. Drawn to something mysterious and simple, I spent my days from morning to night in nature rather than with people. And when I listened to the words people used and talked with them, I felt that the environment of those who spoke like that was not good. I thought that those who spoke like that must have good hearts, but I felt their hearts resonating. Depending on their depth, I could feel whether that person was speaking from a good position or an evil one. Even as a child, I did not want to be friends with other children. For some reason, my heart did not lean towards them. However, it was not the same for those who devoted themselves to heaven. Just sitting next to them or watching their actions made me feel good. That’s how it was.

There is also this story. There was an elderly woman living in Pyongyang who heard about the teacher from the spirit world and came to find him. She then joined the Unification Church. This elderly woman performed many miracles. She healed patients and made those who could not stand up, stand. This rumor spread throughout every corner of Pyongyang, and many parents from the world flocked to her.  
After one, two, or several years, when she reached a certain stage, God said, "Stop such prayers now." Then one day, a woman came to visit. She was a mother with a son from a wealthy family. Her son was suffering from tuberculosis and was racing against time. She pleaded earnestly, saying she would do anything, so please pray for her son. However, no matter how desperately she asked, it could not be done without God's permission. But hearing her story, the teacher felt pity and could not endure it. He wondered if there was any way to heal him and prayed for a hundred days. He kept his body clean and placed holy water to pray. Until the 99th day, there was no response. Then, on the dawn of the hundredth day, a voice was heard from heaven asking, "Do you really want to save this child?" He replied, "Yes, please heal him." Then the voice asked, "Will you not complain about what I do?" He answered, "Yes." Then the water that was in the cup began to rise. The water surged up. Then he was told, "Do not tell anyone about this water; take it to your son and make him drink it. He will walk."  
So, following that command, he took the water and made his son drink it. It was around 3 AM. After returning home and taking a nap, he woke up to find his eldest son getting up early in the morning, saying, "Mother, my stomach hurts." Then he went into his room and died within 30 minutes. At that moment, the grandmother realized that her son had gone in place of that young man.  
After that incident, the grandmother became mentally unstable. However, God had informed her in advance that her son would be taken in place of that young man. While the grandmother was wandering around half out of her mind, her son clearly appeared before her at a crossroads, asking, "Mother, where are you going? You prayed for that young man, and I was sacrificed in his place. Why are you losing your mind?" He said, "I am in a very good place, a place that I cannot reach, even if I do good as a human and serve heaven."  
He said he was in a good place because he had gone to a place that combined where he was supposed to go and where the young man was supposed to go. They had gone to the place where the purposes of both were fulfilled. However, because his mother cried every day, he could not endure it. So he said, "There is no greater cross than this. If you think of me as your son in such a spoiled way, that is a problem." The grandmother then realized, "Ah! I was wrong." Then her son said again, "If you do not love that young man more than me, it will greatly hinder my development in the spirit world, so please promise to love him more than me." This is a fact. When a person with a heavenly mission prays with responsibility, it happens that way. To perform a special miracle, one must pay a special sacrifice. The teacher also experiences this often. There are times when one wants to forgive someone, but cannot do so before heavenly law; however, if one forgives out of compassion, they get caught. Such things happen.
