(Laughter) Everyone else would style their hair with pomade or something. They would say it was because the wind or a typhoon would blow their hair. However, the teacher did not do that. Regardless of whether it was a spring or summer day, he never applied anything. Also, when walking, he never looked up more than 45 degrees from below. He did such things.  
The teacher thought about the various boarding houses he had stayed in before and visited one of them. He met the landlady there. On snowy days or during typhoons, the teacher did not go to school but went out to work at the meal places for lower-class workers. During those times, he felt truly good. Even when a typhoon was blowing, his hands became black, but the rain washed them clean. He worked while sweating in such conditions. That feeling was truly refreshing.  
And if there were bad people among them, he would scold them. The teacher remembers such things well. Sometimes he would take down a big guy. There was a foreman in the labor board who exploited them, taking 30%. So he would strongly protest, saying, "That cannot be done." The teacher would say, "Even if they are scary, that should not be allowed," and he did not follow their words. When the teacher said, "Hey!" they would say, "Ah!" and surrender. He did such things well.  
The teacher suffered a lot of torture from the Japanese. However, after the war ended, he gathered friends who were planning revenge against the special high police officer who tortured them and said, "The pitiful one is defeated Japan. Those who hit those who have already lost their sovereignty and are kneeling and begging will be punished by God." He also quietly called Japanese people who were being chased in Korea and told them to go back quickly before they were tortured, helping them pack. There were many such incidents.  
And the teacher never spoke to people about what kind of thoughts he had. His friends did not know either. The teacher studied the Bible and read religious books and philosophical texts that ordinary people do not usually read.  
There was a friend attending Waseda University who was studying communism, and the teacher had a heated debate with him. He also once gave a loud speech on the street. When the cherry blossoms were in full bloom and many people gathered, he spoke there too. He criticized that era. He shouted, "The youth of tomorrow must proceed in this way." What he prophesied then is now all coming true. At that time, friends who were just wandering around watching would wonder who that young man was, so passionately appealing.  
However, the teacher was silent in the classroom. Because he was silent, no one knew about him. His classmates feared the teacher more than the school teachers. This was because he usually did not speak. When the teacher started asking questions to the school teacher, it would continue until they could not answer. When the teacher stood up to ask a question, the school teacher's face would turn bright red. Therefore, when I stood up, everyone’s faces turned red. Especially during discussions or debates, the school teacher was not a problem. Friends were not a match either.  
At the elementary school graduation ceremony, there is a time for a speech. It is customary for the students to read a speech to the teachers. I still remember what the teacher passionately appealed at that time when he went up to the podium for the last time. Local dignitaries, including the police chief, the county governor, and the principal, were all gathered there. The teacher was hoping for such an occasion. So he boldly went up to the podium. He said he had something to say and criticized the education of the youth and the school teachers up to that point.  
He said, "This teacher has this character. The history teacher has this personality and thinks this way, so this is the only result." He criticized the teachers. He also criticized the times and said that the responsible people of this era must have such and such resolve. He spoke for nearly an hour, and it became a big issue. No one expected a graduating elementary school student to say such things. So from that time, the teacher was labeled. He was identified by the police.  
The teacher studied what people do not do. He contemplated whether this mouth could do what people cannot do, whether it could endure without eating. After thinking, he had the conviction that he could do it and trained himself. Therefore, until he was thirty years old, he never experienced hunger. Whenever food was brought, he would eat three or four bowls at once. He never experienced hunger to that extent. So one day, he thought, "Let's see how much I can eat." During that wartime, there were food tickets. He had those tickets, so he thought, "Let’s see how many bowls I can eat." He took his friends along. When young people gather, it is truly fun. Everyone would say, "Ten bowls are no problem. Today is your birthday, so eat as much as you want; I will treat you." They would shout loudly. If you go down Takadanobaba, there is a temple, and there are restaurants lined up from there. The teacher ate seven bowls of chicken and egg rice there. After eating seven bowls, he could not turn his neck.
It was more painful than being hungry. I couldn't even move. I used to do such things. However, if you think that the teacher always did it that way, it is a big mistake. The teacher was always hungry. But why did he do that? It was never because there was no food. If one only fills their own stomach, the nation will run away far from them. God also runs away from them. Although I wanted to eat because I was hungry, I thought I had to love my nation and God even more than that. That is the truth and the teacher's creed. For that reason, the teacher never had a time without hunger until he was thirty. When he came out of prison, no matter how much he ate, he could keep eating. For some reason, even when he was full, he wanted to eat to the point of overindulging and dying. No matter how much he filled himself, he never reached a state of saturation. It was always lacking. In this way, he paved the way.

You must love Japan, right? To what extent do you love it? It is hard to measure. However, you do not need to love it too much. First, love the parents who gave birth to you! If your parents' hands become thin, hold those hands and shed tears! If your younger sibling cannot wear good clothes like others, hold onto those clothes and shed tears! Take responsibility for your parents and your siblings! How can someone who cannot do that, who does not have that heart, love their country? It is fundamentally incorrect. We are brothers centered around such standards of parents.

The world of the heart has no borders. Language does not become a barrier. When the teacher comes to Japan, he is not a Korean. He is not a Korean person; he is a heavenly person. Therefore, he is a citizen of heaven.

He walked the road from Takadanobaba to Waseda University twice a day. He walked well. Thinking about that, since he has come to a close place, he wants to walk while reminiscing about the past, and he wants to offer a prayer of gratitude for the prayers he made to God that have now been fulfilled in a corner of Japan. That is how the teacher thinks. If the teacher cannot do that and just goes back, he hopes that you will walk from Takadanobaba to Totsukacho in Waseda with such a heart. The winding roads and the telephone poles there are surely soaked with the teacher's tears.

Organization, Unity, and Action
People live feeling sadness in meeting and parting. And now, we have reached a stage where we cannot help but part from you in Japan. However, at this point, what the teacher thinks is which standard of heart is higher: the standard of heart you had before meeting or the standard of heart after meeting and parting. If the heart you have after meeting is not higher than the heart you had before meeting the teacher, then it is meaningless, and that is what the leaders who are guiding you and the heaven that cares for you and the teacher are worried about.

The Meaning of Meeting and Parting
From this perspective, the question is whether being with you for a few days has truly caused a great wave in your world of heart, or whether it has calmed the waves that were already occurring.

It is not a problem of meeting the teacher. If you have a heart that thinks of the teacher after he has gone, then I hope you will think of the nation even more and fulfill your heavenly responsibilities.

October 9, 1965 (Saturday), Tokyo Church, Japan.
* This statement was made at a farewell gathering before departing for Japan, and it has been translated from the Japanese collection of words, "御言集" (Word Collection), Volume 1 (published on February 21, 1980). The title was added by the editor.

The attitude towards the responsibilities that remain and the degree of those responsibilities is what is at issue. Now, how will we proceed with the return to Japan? This is the question. You should have the conviction that you are children of God, work diligently towards the set goal, and as children of God, calmly overcome any obstacles, and I sincerely hope you will become the final victors.

For the church in Japan to progress further in the future, young people like you are most needed. We need young people who will boldly overcome all difficulties that come in their way and call forth the final victory. However, as the saying goes, it cannot be done solely by the hands of the youth. I have felt this deeply while guiding the church. It is essential for the youth to fight with courage, but there must also be those who watch over the fighting youth and protect the surroundings and environment to support them in various ways.

In the adult ministry, there are men's and women's groups, but especially in Japan, being a land of the sun, we need good women as a good land. Moreover, we need good Adams even more than that. It is the adults who can protect the young people who eat abundantly without any worries. No matter how fertile the land is, it is the rice that actually bears fruit. To prosper the adult ministry beyond that of the women's ministry and to achieve great harvests, we must know how to do so.

Adult members have social status and support children and elderly parents. There may be some social obstacles, but we must overcome them. However, if there are young people among your children, you can move around them. The question for Japan is how united and expanded the adult ministry has become, acting in place of the youth ministry, and how the youth and women's ministries are developing together.

To develop, we need a strong counterpart. We must not forget this in the headquarters or in the local areas, in the evangelism system. To lead any adult, the youth must first become that person's children. Therefore, create an environment where that person can protect you as if you were their own children. Even if they are church leaders, treat them as if they were your father and mother. Thus, while regarding those young people as children, they should use them as intermediaries to establish a new spiritual relationship within families and tribes.

I am living with such faith now. Truly, unless we bring about such changes, we cannot be saved. We cannot save Japan either. What is the current state of Japan? If we relate it to China, Russia, or the world situation, what will be Japan's position in the future? To save Japan, we need such ideals and such truths. If you do not practice the truth, what will happen to you? You must not think of it as someone else's problem.

In this case, parents will love their entire family diligently, so they will receive questions of heart. If they do not fulfill their responsibilities as parents, what will happen to their children? When their own child faces a dangerous state due to illness, they must think back to that pain and that heart at that moment and realize that they must educate their children properly, leading them to think for the first time, "Ah! That's right. I must send my young daughter to church." They cannot endure without thinking this way. And when they return from evangelism, they must write a letter. A single letter is simple, but it leaves a genuine exchange of hearts.

They may think they have forgotten that. Humans have intelligence, so the first time they meet someone, they feel that person has a certain kindness and sense of responsibility towards them. No one has treated them like that until now. The closest person to them may treat them kindly as if they were drinking together, but they have never treated them with such a penetrating emotion. Ah, I see I was wrong.

So, they write a letter. And as they visit one person, then another, then another, they gradually become more familiar. When they reach such a relationship, even if they do not repeat what they did during their visits, it will still be fine.

In this way, we must firmly establish the activities and goals of the adult ministry. 

Do you understand, adult members? The teacher thinks like this. Ah, if there were more unified saints, we could create a church for university students, a church for high school students... And a church where only graduates of university and women gather would move greatly if actively promoted. And I think we must particularly develop the adult ministry, so those of you who are of that age should especially work together to develop the adult ministry. Is that alright? If you think it is weak with just men, I hope you will work together to develop the adult ministry with both men and women. If that happens, there are things I want to do centered around Japan. Japan is currently only young people, and we must enter a stage where we must resolve the final issues, so there must be more adults than youth. While a process is needed to reach the goal, it is indeed the adults who will solve the final issues.

The Necessity of Organization
It is easy to fight, but fulfilling responsibilities is not easy. Peter and others were quite old. There were older people, but there were also young and adult people. When this creates an environment of up and down, left and right, front and back, inside and outside, it will lead to remarkable development. Keep this in mind, and the adult members must work hard, praying to establish a foundation that moves with more than one-third of Japan's branches and stems. We are not only aiming for Japan. We are aiming for the world. To do that, it cannot be done by one person. One person cannot do everything. Everyone must work together.

No matter how great the principle is, the principle itself cannot do anything. The problem arises because there are people. And one person alone cannot do this or that. It can only be done when everyone communicates and sets a common goal, fulfilling 100% of their responsibilities in each sector. In the process of becoming, the issue of organization arises. There is a need for a relationship that can connect the entire movement of the church. To make relationships visible, organization becomes an issue. It branches out in all directions like branches centered around a trunk. When that happens, a command system becomes necessary. Without it, one will either find it difficult to manage themselves or cease to exist altogether. Therefore, we need organization.

The teacher must go, leaving you behind. And Nishikawa (최봉춘) must go to America. In that case, Kubo must take responsibility. When thinking about that, what the teacher wants to emphasize the most is to strengthen the organization and establish close relationships with each other. At that time, if you see that one person is responsible, everyone will have different perspectives. The person in charge is one, but there will be a hundred different criticisms. Since the perspectives of the goals differ, the perspectives of criticism will also naturally differ. If the perspective of the goal is different, it cannot ultimately become one. Therefore, if that person is the central leader of a hundred people, they are carrying the burdens of a hundred people. If they stand in the position of 1 out of 100, they must not forget that they must fulfill their mission from their position while carrying 99% of the cross. Do you understand what I am saying?

One cannot just leave the 99 behind and speak as if they are 1. Stand in the position of carrying the 99 and speak. This is the issue. To do that, one must not be just one. In other words, the leader represents 100 and carries the cross of 100 while trying to fulfill their responsibilities, but if you are 1 out of 100, no, you are not, you are the one closest to the leader, so while the leader has the responsibility of 100, each person has the responsibility of 99, standing in for 99 people, treat the leader from that perspective. From that perspective, receive commands. If you move with that heart, you cannot help but become one.

If you do not stand in that position, the leader's opinions will not reach the very front. Therefore, the church leader has the responsibility of 100 people, I have the responsibility of 99 people, with that mindset, the mindset of thinking I am worse than anyone else... Why? Because I could not help carry the cross of 99 people, when you stand in that position, when you could not help carry the cross, you will feel that you are at fault! By taking the overall responsibility as your own, and if you are the one who criticizes yourself, that person will surely become the second leader. Then, why do we create such organizations?

This is for the first leader and the second leader. 

If we do not forget that we need this organization to complete numerous second leaders centered around the first leader, the church in Japan will experience remarkable development.

Once a responsibility is taken, that person becomes the representative of the teacher. If anything happens, the decision-making power at that time lies with that person in charge. All the materials needed to make that decision will be gathered by the surrounding people. It is essential that only the person in charge makes decisions based on those materials. To make such significant decisions, the person with the responsibility must pray earnestly. They must not act according to their feelings or thoughts. Since they are trying to make significant decisions regarding God's work, God will surely work here, but He will also work with the person in the opposing position. The person in charge has the significant responsibility of having to make such comprehensive decisions, and if you help in solving such significant issues closely with the person in charge, you will become the closest person to them. You will become the closest branch.

If everyone is like that, you will not collapse no matter where you are sent. If you go with that standard, you can develop a true organization from there, wherever you go from now on. I sincerely hope you will unite and fulfill such a significant mission. 

Three Essential Elements to Move the World
The headquarters has already become narrower. When there is an event like this, contact the whole country. All the brothers across the country will want to gather. However, that cannot be done. At that time, you must distinguish between the types of people who gather; sometimes these people gather, and sometimes those people gather. If you do not do that, things will not work out.

What? I have been in the Unification Church for a long time, and you are calling someone else instead of me? You must not think that way. During special events, calling the reliable ones is less effective than calling the opposite people. You must not complain about various positions. When you are organized and mobilized, it must be your motto of life to move innocently, and it must be the motto of your life. The teacher speaks this because he feels that this training has not yet been established.

The headquarters gives orders to train you. Therefore, you must gratefully accept all kinds of issues. If you do not have that mindset, it will be a big problem. Otherwise, you will not be able to act in Japan, nor will you be able to move the world. Therefore, the connectivity of the organization, or the ability to govern, is more important than anything else, and it is necessary to obey that.

Thus, the first is organization, the second is unity, and the third is action. These are the three essential elements to move the world centered around Japan. By serving within a thorough organizational authority, we must achieve 100% communication in all directions, and then...
To fulfill our central mission, we must take the lead and establish these standards. One must determine their position, their place within the organization. Without a position, there is no place to sit. One can only work after deciding their position. Depending on one’s efforts, one will realize how significantly that position can grow. Determining one’s position is crucial in strengthening organizational power. 

For an existence to be present in this universe, the issues of front and back, left and right, and up and down must be resolved. If these three do not connect, they will gradually drift apart. If that happens, one’s position will collapse. Once a position is determined, the relationship with the upper and lower levels becomes an issue. In a family, my superior is my father, and above my father is my grandfather. A father must be a great father not only for his son but also to raise a wonderful son in the future. To be a great father, one must study. It is not just for personal success or advancement; it is to become a great father. By leaving such thoughts for one’s descendants and educating them, that lineage can easily sustain Japan.

Marriage is not for oneself. It is to become a great father and mother and to fulfill one’s filial duties. It is done based on that purpose. And if the relationships of up and down, left and right, and front and back do not combine together with one hundred percent unity, that position will shift. When thinking this way, is there anyone in this world standing centered around such a nation? No. Is there anyone in the religious world standing in such a position centered around the teachings and doctrines of their religion? No. Each person is seeking their desired position, losing the center, and collapsing. If that happens, one cannot compete in this world.

The need for organization is to determine one’s position. One must not be unaware of their position. Do you understand? Determining one’s position is for forming connections and relationships. It must be centered around oneself. The one who has the authority to connect becomes the subject. The one receiving guidance becomes the counterpart. Therefore, if one establishes such a relationship and determines their position, that is, if one connects in all directions and determines their position, they can stand firmly regardless of the direction—front, back, left, or right.

The universe is interconnected. Even God cannot be harmed by this. It must not happen otherwise. After determining one’s position, one must unify all relationships concerning oneself within that multidimensional sphere. One must be nurtured with such driving force. Therefore, if one needs organization, they must determine their position. To determine a position, one must create a subject circle. To create a subject circle, one must establish a counterpart centered around oneself and then create that circle; otherwise, it cannot exist as a single entity forever. It will collapse. The position will naturally become extinct.

When organizational power and unity become one, only then can action be taken. When the center does such things, saying, “It has nothing to do with me. You go west. I will go east,” it will soon fall into a state of destruction. Therefore, organization, unity, and action are all elements of societal development.

Thus, everything must be quickly established based on the criteria of determining such positions toward that purpose, so that relative standards can be set for the whole to become unified. Unified action must be taken. If not, it will prosper nowhere. That is the principle. In the case of executing national policies in Japan, first, each must determine the organization they stand in, decide their position within that organizational power, and smoothly establish relationships in all directions, leading to a royal path from a subjective position, where there will be development.

If one does not stand in such a position, they will center around one person. This leads to crisis or disorder. It is not about taking responsibility for the nation but rather pursuing one’s own goals. Therefore, you must clearly distinguish this and enter the organizational power to determine your position.

Moving positions and thereby losing relationships is the root of corruption. Acting contrary to God’s word is the beginning of corruption. Therefore, it is clear that one must know their position and enter the organizational power to establish relationships. To do this, one must certainly stand in a relative position. One must demonstrate the unity that can act as a heavenly force there. I hope you always keep this in mind and do not forget it. Do you understand?

First, what? Organization. Why organization? To determine positions. Second, what? Unity. Based on the criteria of that determined position, one must determine the position of the counterpart concerning the subject. When that happens, they become one. To become one, there must be a common purpose and a direction toward one world. It must not be otherwise. There must be unified action toward the purpose. Nothing can be done outside of this principle. Then, one can clearly know who is above. If you forget this hierarchical relationship, nothing can be done.

Who is above? Who is the ultimate? Centering around the family, it is one’s father and one’s children. The front and back relationship is with oneself and one’s spouse; the left and right relationship is with siblings. Expanding that scope leads to such a position. Men and women are in a front and back relationship. Speaking of a teacher, the front and back relationship is with me and all of you. Broadly speaking, everyone is included. Therefore, center yourself, and let your mind and body become one. Move your arms left and right. Advance forward and backward through that. Or engage in historical actions. And leave a name. What is left returns to the descendants. That is the relationship.

The universe is interconnected. One must clearly understand this. Anything that opposes this is fundamentally not tolerated. In cases of opposition, there can be no development, growth, or progress. Cell division—what divides? When the relationships in all directions are perfectly established, and when a new cell tries to emerge, if there is no place to relate, it seeks a new standard elsewhere to reproduce a new cell. I hope everyone does not forget this principle.

Then, you can immediately know what position you are taking and what actions you are performing. Is it on the side of Satan or on the side of God? You have no right to interfere with your superiors. If a leaf complains to the stem, “Stem! Stem! Stem!” what will happen? Without the stem, the leaf will die. Therefore, who can question the stem? Only the root can. The root can rightfully admonish the stem. This is because it is within the root's responsibility.

If one acts contrary to the principle, they must develop this further. If one’s superior makes a mistake, they must strive to save them, even at the cost of their own sacrifice. If not, both will perish. One must save at least one. To do this, even if one must cut off the branch itself, they must save the stronger side. This is the principle. This is somewhat difficult for individuals within the modern democratic ideology.

If everyone stands on their own standards, saying, “You are you, and I am I,” the world will split apart. It will split apart, and in the end, there will be nothing that can be done, and ultimately it will collapse. Thus, modern civilization ends up concluding everything through oneself.

If one acts contrary to the principle, they will naturally face such consequences. Therefore, a branch must not complain about the stem. To save the stem, one must be willing to perish. This is sacrifice. Thus, in Eastern thought, there is the concept of loyalty. In the West, this is currently not accepted. However, at some stage, since humanity has fallen, there is no way to proceed without doing so. If not, both the fallen and the unfallen will ultimately weep.

Where are you? If you are a branch, what kind of branch are you? Are you a branch in the east, a branch in the west? Or are you in the south or the north? Regardless of which direction you are in, if you say to the center, “What are you?” the tree will die. Unless everyone reaches the standard of the center, one cannot stand in the complete purpose sphere. Therefore, everyone must organize around the headquarters and must not cut off the central stem.

If one has the intention to cut, that is not a mindset of principled criticism. To criticize, one must know their position, unity, and strength, and such directional positions. If centered around oneself, there will be no roots or stems, and one will turn to ashes. That is what happened to Satan. Because he left his position, he became the protagonist pushing everything into the realm of death. One must clearly understand this and know what path we are taking.

Once this is clearly resolved, one must not abandon the concept of the church center and their personal emotional issues. Are you speaking on behalf of ten people, or are you speaking to make ten people your allies? Which side will be recognized as the center? If you cannot judge there, then change direction to another. If your own thoughts chase you, it is better to close the window and sleep.

Therefore, we must thoroughly secure our positions to protect ourselves from Satan, who aims to invade us whenever there is a gap, and we must reach the ultimate purpose of victory. Even if we must die a hundred times, we must go. One must think of the fate of that world. One must clearly understand these standards. Then, one will know how to move in such an organization.

Thus, organization, unity, action. There is only one position that determines that. If there are two, the world will become two. This is a responsibility that must be fulfilled even if God stakes eternity on it, and if the teacher bears that responsibility, you must also bear that responsibility. It is a painful matter. The fact that we are already born is not recognized by God, but we are within some organizational power. I am also connected and have relationships within that power. What will happen to the actions we are currently taking? One must not skip a step. In this world, each person has the path of the cross remaining. Each must cross over that path of death.

That is the individual’s cross, and as the church moves toward society, it manifests as a cross, or when Japan tries to move toward the world, it appears as a cross, and you must bear that global cross. You must not forget that there is a cross waiting for you in the front. You, standing right in front of it, must advance with courage and confidence.

How are you doing? Next, I will talk about issues within the church and your issues. What is the relationship between Cain and Abel? Do you know? Absolutely, standing on the heavenly path, Abel must obey any command given day or night and act one hundred percent accordingly. If one stands in such a position, they are completely alive. What is alive grows. This is the principle.

Therefore, one must observe themselves from the perspective of whether they are alive or not and must always be cautious. Watching young people is pleasant, but on the other hand, it brings much worry. Even Adam, who was the only son of God, fell. Are you standing in a position better than Adam? Not at all. The elements that can lead to a fall are scattered around you by dozens or hundreds. Always keep your eyes on the good and quickly surpass this limit.

If one does not tread on the principles, they will fly into the Pacific Ocean. Do you know what it means to fly into the Pacific Ocean? You must fight as well. At that time, if you must whip to create good people, that is not evil. If Satan whips to take good people to his side, that is the utmost evil. However, striking Satan, the utmost evil, with God’s whip and placing them in the position of the heavenly prince is good. One must understand this in reverse.

If one does not listen, they may be struck with a whip. They may strike the delinquents or the lazy in Japan or those who disturb society. When wishing for Japan, it is not because of my own desires but because of the desire for the world. One must not forget that. Therefore, when you see the teacher, “Ah, that teacher is a teacher from Korea, but wanting Japan is bad from a national perspective.” Thinking like this is problematic. Wanting Japan is because one wants the world. Wanting the world is wanting the heavenly sovereignty, and wanting the heavenly sovereignty is to make God our God.

Japan, Korea, compete. Japan, do not lose. Korea, do not lose. America, do not lose. Win quickly. Japan is needed to love the world. Japan is needed to save the world. Those who need it cannot be placed in a comfortable position. They stand in the world. They are washed by the great waves. They must be hit. Why? To ride the waves of the world, one must be hit. If one dislikes that, they should run away. If one is such a weakling, they are not needed.

Do you have the confidence to accomplish such things? I want to walk on every part of Japan with my own feet. In Korea, there is no place the teacher has not gone. And with tears, I stepped on that land, thinking of saving that good country. The path taken for ten years, twenty years does not change. No matter how the waves crash, I stand firm. Like a rock. A large rock may be washed for tens of millions of years, but it stands firm. The harder it becomes, the closer it resembles its original form. The weaker it is, the more holes it has.

How are you doing? Do you not have holes? The Unification Church acts on conviction. Those who have become one will remain as they are, no matter how many thousands or tens of thousands of years pass. I hope to quickly make all of Japan a country that aligns with God’s will.

If you do not do it, the teacher may come and do it. However, you will say, “Please let me do it.” Therefore, the teacher intends to leave the cloth with you and return. And after returning once, he will check how things have turned out.

But there were holes, teacher! This cloth had holes, so everything leaked out. This must not happen. If there are holes, take the cloth yourself and think that it is a cloth that can last for a thousand or ten thousand years. If the holes become large, sew them up. If there is no fabric and it is really difficult, stick anything on it. If you cannot carry it on your shoulder, bring it all to a rock and place it there. And let it be packed at the end.

The path of restoration. It is not to destroy Japan. Our position is to save Japan. To do this, there must be first organization, second unity, and third unified action.
must be taken. By doing so, the emotional issues will naturally be resolved among you. The teacher hopes for this and will return with a joyful heart. The teacher is very happy to return. You feel the same way, right? Do not feel sad, but be filled with hope when the teacher returns. 

My primary purpose 
has failed in the plan. I feel ashamed. I have no face to meet the teacher. However, from now on, I hope to change this shameful appearance and present myself with dignity. I sincerely wish to establish the purpose of my own face in heaven and earth. 

Until now, I have talked about the church, but this time I would like to focus on you. In order to achieve victory, restoration does not start from oneself. It comes from the outside. When God created, He did not create from Himself. Everything, including all creation, was made starting from the most fundamental basis. Restoration is a process of re-creation. Therefore, it is the path of restoration to love the enemies whom one cannot love after placing one's beloved family behind. Satan loved. If you do not write a certificate stating that, you cannot go to where your parents are and love them. This is a principle, so God has sacrificed His most beloved children until now. The place that heaven and earth must surely reach 
I thank God for being with us on this long journey, and I sincerely appreciate that you all prayed so much for our safe return. 

During the time I traveled around the world, I saw many new facts and encountered many new things. I cannot tell you everything at this time. Therefore, I will postpone those stories for later, and at this time, I would like to talk about the fields we must go forward in based on what I felt while traveling the world. 

I will speak briefly on the topic of "The Place that Heaven and Earth Must Surely Reach." Since the venue is narrow, it may be quite uncomfortable, but please create an atmosphere of grace quietly together. 

The direction and purpose God is heading 
Today, whether it is individuals, families, our country, or even the entire world, we all acknowledge that we must not remain in our current lives and environments. What does this mean? Originally, God existed, and He had a purpose in His providence, and if things had gone according to His will, the reality we see today would not have occurred. 

If this has happened despite God's existence, we must acknowledge the involvement of some other being that is not God. Therefore, we cannot deny the fact that we are living in a fallen world today. In other words, because we are fallen, we must not deny the reality and must have the mission of pioneers and the mission of fighters towards a new hope for tomorrow, and we cannot deny the historical destiny and the practical circumstances that require us to go through the path of struggle and adversity. 

God cannot leave this world as it is. Therefore, leading countless humans on earth, the steps taken until now towards the place that heaven and earth must go is the history of humanity and the history of providence that we know well. 

Originally, there should have been a society and world that God had providentially established and that fulfilled God's hope, a homeland that all people could share. In that homeland, we should have established a foundation of heart, formed relationships with loving parents, and that parents...
It is undeniable that the central theme of establishing a relationship among brothers, forming a single family, clan, tribe, nation, and ultimately creating a new world is what humanity demands and desires today, and it was God's original purpose of creation. The reason this purpose has not been achieved in the world is due to our human ancestors making mistakes because of Satan's temptation. Therefore, we are fighting to break free from this environment. We can see from the historical course that the reason God has fought until now is also found here.

From this perspective, we can understand that God has sought out Korea until now. Furthermore, we can recognize that He has also sought out many nations and ethnic groups scattered across the world. There remains a path that God must continue to pursue. We know well that God is in a position where He must guide humanity toward a final goal, and that He is the one who must lead that humanity.

Heaven has sought out the earth, and humanity is following the purpose that Heaven desires. However, although the purposes of Heaven and humanity should align and share the same direction, we have yet to see a point of agreement in purpose or direction throughout the historical process. Thus, many ancestors have labored throughout history, but their efforts did not become labors for the purpose, nor did they become a foundation for the eternal and unchanging victory of Heaven's will, but rather flowed away without achieving that.

When we look at the history of the Israelite people, we see that in the family of Adam, centered around Abel and Cain, God sought Abel as a point of hope to establish the great original purpose of Heaven. However, Abel, who encountered God's providence in that historical course, could not bear it and thus could not accept God who was coming to him. Moreover, because he did not prepare the necessary foundation before God, a conflict arose between Cain and Abel, causing the purpose and direction of God, who had come to Abel's family, to go awry.

When we think of God today, we realize that it is not because we demanded it that God has come to us, but rather that God has come to us because He desires it. It is human beings who should not be in such a position, and it is the mission and responsibility of fallen humanity to escape from such an environment. It is our inherent duty to welcome the One who has come, and if there are difficulties in the path He takes, it is our mission to remove them; yet we must recognize that among our ancestors, there was not a single one who fulfilled this.

Abel himself did not know the path that God was taking, nor did he prepare a foundation to welcome God. Abel himself did not align with God's purpose and direction, and even though Cain and Abel were brothers, they fought against each other, causing God's direction and purpose to deviate at that time.

Thus, God sought Noah again. Although Noah labored for 120 years, we must understand that behind that labor was God, who worked even harder than Noah. 

In that long span of 120 years, with countless enemies mocking him and no one to welcome him, we must recognize how heart-wrenching it must have been for God to watch Noah, who followed the time and purpose that God longed for.

Noah himself did not know the steps that God was taking, nor did his family know the path that Noah should follow. 

In this way, all individuals, families, or those who were connected to God's providence throughout history have failed to fulfill their responsibilities before God's will, causing God to experience sorrow. Because Noah's family could not fulfill God's will, the providence was extended again through Abraham, passing through Moses to Jesus, covering a long history of 4,000 years, during which God came with the mission of a pioneer. 

For 4,000 years, and even until now, we must recognize how much effort God has made to establish the chosen people of Israel while looking forward to that one day that had not yet been achieved. 

For 4,000 years, God has continually labored, and He has been constantly rejected, never able to rest peacefully. Our ancestors and the ancestors of Israel should reflect on the fact that during the time when God was grieving and suffering, they did not comfort Him but rather betrayed Him. 

Throughout 4,000 years, among the betraying nations, there was not a single representative who could welcome God, nor was there anyone who could represent a nation that could express gratitude for God's labor, nor anyone who could stand as a central being capable of comforting God's suffering, aligning with God's purpose and direction to fulfill that purpose. We know that this central being was Jesus Christ, whom God sent after 4,000 years of labor.

Jesus came as the one who would resolve God's sorrow on behalf of 4,000 years of history and was the one who came to align God's purpose and direction. However, the Israelite people failed to follow His direction and inherit His purpose, and they did not correct their past mistakes in line with His goals. As a result, Jesus had to face a time of historical sorrow that could not proceed without Him. This remains an unspeakable and painful truth for humanity today.

For this reason, even after Jesus came and went, God remains in a position where He must bear the historical course of labor and fulfill the mission of a pioneer. Therefore, we must not forget how many tears and sweat God has shed behind the scenes to bring about the global development we see today.

When we look at the history of Christianity, we must be grateful for all the prophets and ancestors who have shed blood to broaden the foundation toward the purpose that God desires. However, we must also recognize that every time God faced these individuals, longing for a time of hope, His heart was filled with indescribable sorrow as He watched them go to their deaths with earnestness and devotion. Furthermore, we must understand that God's greater sorrow was that the Israelite nation, which had labored for 4,000 years to lay the foundation, was shattered, and He had to use foreign nations to restore it.

God has been calling people until now. Until now, God has also borne the mission of a pioneer. We must reflect on the fact that there has not been a true group or a true existence that has paved the way to welcome God and prepared a foundation to bring Him rest on this earth.

As we consider God's position today, we must recognize that the miserable history of Christianity hidden within the 2,000 years has been a history that has caused God to labor and suffer. 

For this reason, Christianity must not be divided into numerous denominations. It must become one. The upper and lower, left and right, front and back must be united in the mission and purpose of God's providence, regardless of the era or period. This was the mission of the followers of Christianity. However, they have been dragged along in history without knowing where God's direction lies or what His purpose is. If they had aligned with God's purpose and direction, Christianity would not be in such a powerless state today.

On this earth, we must align with God's purpose and direction, prepare an environment where God can come, and establish the way of filial piety and the law of loyalty before Him. The one who came as the responsible figure for this was Jesus. However, He left without being able to express the feelings He held within.

Looking at Heaven, we see that God's great labor remains, and looking at the earth, we see that there are still wandering masses. Jesus Christ realized that He must return to guide the wandering humanity on earth and comfort God. For this reason, Jesus placed the term "Second Coming" at some future goal and promised to return. Therefore, He urged us to become brides who are fully loyal to God and commanded us to be children who are fully loyal to Him. He instructed us to cultivate the way of loyalty toward God.

However, because a point from which we can start with God and Jesus has not been established centered on this earth, the world has become one we do not desire, and Christianity has not become the Christianity that God and Jesus require, continuing to roll along in this reality that we know well is coming to an end.

At this juncture, as we reflect once more, we must ask what kind of person God is calling to this earth. God is not calling those with great knowledge, nor those with authority to command the world.

If the path God is taking is the path of the cross, He will call those who can make that path level. If that path is a thorny road, He will call those who can bear the responsibility of a pioneer on that thorny road.

God does not desire those who wish for Him to come centered on themselves; rather, He desires those who can comfort the sorrow and pain of God, who has labored for 6,000 long years, by fulfilling the duties of loyal subjects and dutiful children. Therefore, we must decide to stand as true children who can establish the emotional standard of God, which has never existed throughout history. This is the historical destination that humanity must ultimately reach today.

Even at this moment, we carry within us the grief that cannot be resolved, crying out toward Heaven. We are also struggling day and night to fulfill the mission of a pioneer that others do not know. If my strength is lacking today, I must take my vows as a condition of faith and dedicate everything I have, becoming the one who will pave the way that God must go.

A person who can truly comfort God

Throughout 6,000 years of history, many groups and denominations have come forth demanding their own salvation and rest from God, but our Unification Church cannot do that.

Feeling ashamed that we cannot establish our own face and reputation before the God who has come until now, we must become the vanguard that pioneers the thorny path and the way of Golgotha left in this nation and the world, shouldering the foundation of labor that God must bear. I must be able to walk the thorny path that God must take.

Therefore, if we cannot become a group that can provide a moment of rest and a day of rest for God when He comes, we will face the question of where God will go.

Even when looking at the historical currents and empirical facts today, in this age where individualism is prevalent, it is becoming increasingly difficult to find someone willing to present themselves as a sacrificial offering before the whole. This phenomenon is evident in all aspects of society, and under such social conditions, God cannot come.

Thus, we must resolutely determine to be the guide for the One who is pioneering the path that God will labor on. We must be those who worry that the dirty soil may stain the clothes He wears. We must not become a source of worry before Him.

In preparing the path for the One who comes, if there are any mistakes in our pledge of loyalty to God, it has been the responsibility of countless religious individuals to find a group among humanity that can say, "You should not do that," and worry together. However, when we look at the world, we can clearly feel that we are moving further away from that realm and deviating from the original trajectory.

The members of the Unification Church have the responsibility to establish a victory on earth by capturing the direction based on the ideal of creation. If we are to suffer for God, we must pledge our loyalty and become a man or woman who can practice that pledge of loyalty.

God has a hope for one purpose and intention, and there are circumstances that must be confronted on the earth, and He has feelings that must be connected to us. If we are to take on the path where God's desires, circumstances, and feelings are intertwined, we cannot stop the path we have been taking until now, and we must create conditions under which God can willingly command us.

The conditions under which God can command us must not be absent from the historical course of this era. We must become those who volunteer to receive orders from our Father.

Jesus prayed in the Garden of Gethsemane, "My Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me; nevertheless, not as I will, but as you will." (Matthew 26:39) From this, we can see that there was a distance between Jesus and God's will. The circumstances were different. The emotional standards were different. That is why He prayed, "Not as I will, but as you will." The Father's will is the absolute purpose that Heaven and earth must pursue. It is essential that a person arises to fulfill that purpose.

For this reason, God has established the way to serve Him as a model that humanity must find and realize in a position where their ideology, emotions, and lives can align, through countless prophets throughout history and through Jesus. Nevertheless, we know that humans have continued with vague distances and uncertain faith until now.

At this present moment, God is demanding responsibility from us. Therefore, when you move forward for the purpose, how you go is important. You must not stand in the position of dying like Abel, nor in the position of undermining Noah's overall purpose like Ham, nor in the position of making mistakes with the three offerings like Abraham. You must not enter the environment where Moses struck the rock incorrectly or where Jesus prayed in the Garden of Gethsemane, "My Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me."

So, what should you center on? You must find a more solid center than the position of Jesus. This is the end time.

We are to pioneer the world centered on Jesus, who has the mission of a pioneer.
You must be able to step forward and say that you will take on what has been done. Jesus wanted to go and save all the people of the world, but He could not. He could not take responsibility before God, who comes to this earth, and pave the way. We must know in advance the path that God will take and prepare that way, so that He can come and rest here.

I have not been able to go to the position where I can do so. Therefore, Jesus had to bear a grudge and could not help but go. 

So what is the ultimate point that heaven and earth demand? It is a point where God comes to find me, and I cannot go, nor can I do anything; that is, I must take responsibility for the path God will take and the work He will do, and I must provide a foundation to give God rest. This must be paved on this earth. 

How should this be done? The path that God has worked hard on for 6,000 years has not been a path of glory. God has shed blood and sweat for the sake of all people, trying to save them even on the path of death. However, even while being constantly rejected by humanity, God has sought such an environment and has worked tirelessly to fulfill the mission of a pioneer, which Jesus understood well. 

When Jesus carried the cross and headed toward Golgotha, despite being struck down repeatedly, He said, "Father, forgive them," feeling that it was frustrating to fall. He went on this path with the heart that he could not fulfill his filial duty before God, falling twelve times and each time thinking, "I am going this way because I could not dedicate my blood to my Father and could not fulfill my filial duty." Because of this heart, Satan could not establish a condition for accusation before God. 

Before Jesus, who devoted Himself to God and gave His life, even Satan could not accuse Him. Thus, we know that the new resurrection took place, and the Christian faith began. Therefore, the father cannot leave the son, nor can the child separate from the father; this is the heavenly principle. 

And so, the one who comes to fulfill the will that could not be achieved on this earth is the returning Jesus. He will come to this earth to teach how to comfort God and how to take responsibility on behalf of God, as well as the duties of a child. Thus, the victorious being who can eliminate all activities and conditions that God does not demand, that is, the central being that God requires, will be able to manage all environments.

Until now, the workers of unification may find that meeting the teacher may become a regretful experience. I know that you have walked a path of adversity that no one knows about. Among you, there may be those who have followed with joy and those who have followed reluctantly due to circumstances. There will be various forms. However, the question is whether each of you can fulfill the historical mission entrusted to you from your respective positions, align your direction with the purpose that heaven and earth equally demand, and at the same time, be able to present conditions of comfort before God. When you think about this, you may feel that you are still far from it. 

Until now, those who believe in Jesus have said, "Oh, God is on the throne, let all creation worship Him." Does it seem that way? When your own sons and daughters are dying at the brink of death and you are in a position to sing a funeral song, can you say, "Oh, you are having fun"? 

If God were such a being, He could only be seen as unrelated to humanity. Just as a child cannot comprehend the heart of a parent in a fallen world, they cannot understand how great the deep heart of the original Father, who created heaven and earth, is toward His children. 

Even if I die a hundred or a thousand times, I must return to God. My desires and hopes must revolve around God, and when you are at ease for a day, I should hope for a year of peace while my Father rests for a thousand years. We must be those who wish to enjoy the joy of a lifetime because of Him when He sings glory for countless ages. 

God does not desire Christians who live their faith centered around their own denominations. The teacher also has the signboard of the Unification Church, but he thinks about when he can take this sign down. 

You may be receiving attention as members of the Unification Church, but the question is when that attention will disappear from the Korean Peninsula. Our members scattered around the world are striving with a determination to resolve God's deep sorrow and are running with a heart of loyalty and devotion to take on God's path of suffering. The group that resolves to fall while doing this is the members of the Unification Church. This path is a blessed path. 

However, when looking at the world, Christians believe that the returning Jesus will come again before the Israelite people, or that He will come to the shores of the Sea of Galilee or the Mount of Olives. 

God is seeking those who can subdue Satan and fulfill the duty of loyalty and filial piety. God is not crying out of longing for hell. The earth is not the problem. I visited the Mount of Olives this time, and that mountain is not the problem. There must be someone who can move the Mount of Olives and establish the duty of loyalty and filial piety before God. 

The number of Christians is not the issue. What is needed is a person who becomes the body of God and resolves to go anywhere at any time according to God's command, someone whom God would like to command with joy. Among the billions of Christians who boast of their numbers today, can we truly find such a person? If you are threatened with a knife at your side and asked whether you will sacrifice yourself as an offering on the heavenly altar, if you cannot overcome that moment, you are nothing. 

We need people who are willing to risk their lives for the sake of loyalty to God, who can leap into the heavens. I believe such people are the revolutionary army of the end times. 

Today, gathering here does not mean that everything is over. Meeting the teacher may be an important matter, but it should not become the purpose of your faith. You must meet the teacher and then go back. Because God still has a sorrowful path to walk, you must go that way. 

God will seek individuals, families, nations, and states that can fulfill such responsibilities before all of humanity. God has come to find such individuals. Such individuals must comfort God's heart, fulfill the duty of loyalty before Him, and resolve all matters of heaven and earth. Thus, God will say, "You are the one who can take responsibility before this era." When I look at you, I can hope for tomorrow, and when I look at you, I can lead today's battle to victory. 

You must become such an individual. Such individuals are absolutely necessary. 

God must hold onto such individuals and say, "You are bone of my bones, flesh of my flesh, and heart of my heart." No matter how many ancestors there have been in history and how many people there are in the world, you are in the position of the greatest ancestor in history centered on heart. Unless such a being appears on this earth, the history of sorrow caused by the fall of humanity cannot be resolved, and those of us born in that history must again serve some parents. 

The Path of True Parents 

The one who must fulfill the duty of loyalty and filial piety on the emotional foundation of God must create a position that can unify all that God has given and determine the position of parents representing heaven and earth in the emotional world of the Way. That is why Jesus used the terms bride and groom, hoping for such a standard. 

The groom represents the Father. It refers to the standard of the Father who has not fallen. The bride refers to the standard of the Mother who has not fallen. Thus, as true parents who have not fallen, they left the names of bride and groom to achieve the ideal of creation at the end times. 

The bride and groom must unify their hearts. In unifying hearts, the sad heart of God must not be involved. We must eliminate all historical sadness and be able to fulfill the hope of history. Therefore, we must be able to walk the path of fulfillment before the will, increasingly finding ourselves in an environment overflowing with joy day by day. 

Where is the place we must go today, and where must all humanity absolutely go? We must find the place where we can resolve God's sorrow, create days of joy and hope, and stand in the position of our ancestors in terms of emotional standards. If we do not determine such a position, there can be no emotional resting place in this world. If we do not determine that, the foundation of peace and happiness will not appear on this earth. 

From that perspective, the center of love must revolve around the names of the bride and groom. This must be the case because, centered on God, the true ancestors of humanity, that is, the true parents of humanity, can appear. From the perspective of humanity, all non-principled elements arising from non-principled bloodlines must be removed, and we must be reborn and connected again as true parents' offspring. 

What is salvation? Salvation is restoration. It is to subdue Satan, who has violated heaven and earth, centered on God's heart. One must resolve all historical content created centered on Satan and fulfill loyalty and filial piety before God with the ideal heart of the world’s parents, paving the way for happiness before God. Only such a person can unite with God and establish the connection of their children. 

Now humanity must go to find true parents. After that, we must fulfill the duty of loyalty before those true parents. Adam and Eve could not fulfill the duty of loyalty before God. Originally, they should have fulfilled the duty of loyalty to God and then multiplied children, allowing those children to inherit the duty of loyalty. In other words, a tribe centered on the emotional law of God should have appeared. God has been working for 6,000 years to establish such a tribe. 

Thus, in the history of Christianity, an environment of adoption was necessary to establish the duty of the son. The relationship between Cain and Abel must be extended repeatedly to prepare a foundation for restoration that connects global relationships. To establish an individual Abel, a personal Cain is needed; to establish a family Abel, a family Cain is needed; to establish a national Abel, a national Cain is needed; and to establish a global Abel, a global Cain is needed. Thus, they divide into two factions. 

You must understand what an Abel world is. 

Regarding Adam, if there is someone who has the right to judge, saying, "Adam! You have violated God's heart, broken the heavenly principle, and violated the position of being God's child," then that person can also judge all of humanity in history. 

We must find such a person, learn the way from them, and if they are sad, we must also be able to feel their sadness. If God allows that person to determine the way of true parents, we must take on the cross that true parents must bear, and we must fulfill the duty of loyalty and become dutiful sons and daughters. Only then can the tradition be established. 

Even if a typhoon blows and the environment shakes all around, we must firmly hold onto the relationships in all directions and establish an absolute standard that will not be invaded, and only then will God recognize it. Those who are invaded cannot be accepted. 

Where is the place humanity must go today? We must find our hometown. We must go to our hometown and meet our parents. Until now, idealism and various ideologies have all played the role of a staff in that process. But what will we do after meeting our parents? We must become children who can receive 100 percent of our parents' true love. However, because we have not done so, we must go through procedures. The one who comes to teach these procedures is the returning Lord. 

All people must learn the procedures from Him and, by being grafted onto Him, act on His behalf. That is why Jesus referred to Himself as the true olive tree and spoke of the parable of grafting. 

Thus, through true parents, true families, true tribes, and true nations emerge. However, the issue is the true nation. If Jesus had had a nation, He would not have died. If the Israelite people had united and fulfilled the duty of loyalty before Jesus, no matter how much Rome tried to oppress them, they would not have perished. 

After Jesus died, for 400 years, Rome tried to swallow Christianity through deception and oppression, but in the end, it was absorbed in reverse. If Jesus had lived, He would have conquered Rome within 40 years. 

Why was there no family before such Jesus? Jesus had no parents who could be called my father and mother in the homeland. If there is a heavenly presence, there must naturally be one on earth. Jesus had to leave behind a foundation of victory in the battle to declare, "I am your father." And we had to inherit that. However, because Jesus left behind a grudge that could not be fulfilled, He must come again to set the goal of restoration. This is what is regrettable. 

God cannot work centered on you, and in that sense, you cannot help but recognize the work that the teacher is doing. 

Why could Jesus not personally teach the heavenly principles that would allow Him to have parents, that is, God? Originally, if there had been no fall, God would have become Adam's parent, but due to the fall, the relationship between parent and child was severed. Therefore, we must restore the duty of loyalty and filial piety that was not fulfilled due to the severed relationship. Until then, God cannot teach from the position of a parent. 

"Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me," Jesus prayed, but why did God not answer that prayer? What deep grievance was there that salvation could not be established without Jesus' death? "If you do not believe when I speak of earthly matters, how will you believe when I speak of heavenly matters?" What is the story behind Jesus' words? Those ignorant people, who do not understand the times, only think about bread...

You must have the heart that says, "As your heart is like this before you, please encourage me so that I can fulfill the duty of loyalty that can comfort your heart." 

Today, we must once again reflect from such a standpoint.
In order to settle the price of the fall that has caused us to be without parents on this earth, we have reached a critical juncture where we must fight. The Purpose of Salvation. I will speak on the topic of the purpose of salvation. 
A Significant Issue That Must Be Resolved in Our Lifetime 
We are well aware that the world we live in is not a good one. Even when we look at our individual selves living in such a world, we cannot deny that we have factors of conflict within us. In other words, our body and mind are at war. From an environmental perspective, we cannot deny that this is a sinful world, and from our own standpoint, it is undeniable that it is an extremely difficult era to establish any center. 
So why have this world and humanity become like this?
You must discover yourself moving in a consistent direction. This is a significant issue that we must resolve throughout our lives. This problem arose because humanity has fallen. 

Then, how did the path of morality or religion come about? It is to return fallen humanity to its original state before the fall. So, what is salvation in this context? It is returning to the state before illness. This can be contrasted with the noun of restoration. Therefore, salvation is indeed restoration.

What is the fall? It is the loss of one's inherent value. Then, who is the center of that value? God. Therefore, the fall refers to the loss of God, and the loss of the true human value that can always relate to God in a unified position. Additionally, it is the loss of a valuable foundation in the social environment in which humans live. The concept of salvation emerged to determine the original position by finding the value of humanity that can restore this environmental foundation and the heavenly value that can govern such humans.

Now, let us examine the specifics of the fall. At what stage did humanity fall? In the beginning, in the Garden of Eden, God was present, and there was the original human ancestor, Adam and Eve, created by God centered on His purpose of creation, along with the angels who cooperated in God's work centered on that original Adam and Eve.

Then, what were the purposes of God's intention, Adam and Eve, and the angels? It is not something that can be achieved only by the angels living joyfully, nor can it be achieved only by Adam and Eve living joyfully, nor can it be completed by God being joyful alone. When all—God, Adam and Eve, and the angels—achieve their purpose under a common goal, then the angels can rejoice, Adam and Eve can rejoice, and God can also rejoice. It cannot be that only one side rejoices. In other words, it must be that God, the center of heaven and earth, and Adam and Eve, who represent heaven and earth, along with the angels who represent the environment, can all rejoice together. Only when the purpose of creating humanity is fulfilled can the purpose of salvation, that is, the original purpose of creation, be achieved.

However, that purpose has been shattered. The standard has fallen. When it fell, in what order did it fall? It did not start from God. It began to fall from the opposing position. This is the order of the fall.

To restore what has fallen, since it fell in this order, how should it be restored? It must be aligned through the opposite path of providence. In this way, it is the path of restoration that seeks to find a loyal servant who can represent the true archangel of the heavenly world on this earth.

What then is an angel? An angel is a being that must fulfill the duty of loyalty before God from the position of a servant and must serve as a protective fence for Adam and Eve. The purpose of God creating the angels was for Adam and Eve. That is the purpose for which the archangel was created.

Here, what must remain until the very end? The spirit world must be reorganized into a world like the angelic world that can focus solely on heaven, and a new parent centered on Cain and Abel, who can focus solely on heaven, must be established on this earth.

This is the Cain-type world and the Abel-type world. Heaven has created it this way.

To have dominion over all things is a blessing that God bestowed upon Adam and Eve, His children. In other words, it is the content of God's blessing to humanity. **Purpose of Salvation**

**The Position and Mission of John the Baptist**

Today, Christian believers say that Jesus will return riding on clouds with the sound of the archangel's trumpet, but that is not the case. The representative central being of that mission was John the Baptist. Therefore, he said, "Repent, for the kingdom of heaven is at hand! I have come not for myself, but to bear witness to Him."

John the Baptist came as a servant to represent the entire nation of Israel and had to restore the position of Adam right after the fall. He had to restore the position that could connect to the position of Adam before the fall. The representative who had to promise to restore the position of the unfallen Adam in this fallen world and inherit all authority was John the Baptist.

The statement "Repent, for the kingdom of heaven is at hand" was not just John's personal statement. It represented the entire history of Israel, the Israelite nation, 4,000 years of history, and all of humanity living on this planet. Furthermore, the position where John the Baptist baptized Jesus was the position of inheriting all historical responsibilities. From that point on, Jesus would begin His mission.

What does this mean? It means that a heavenly loyal servant has not yet emerged on this earth. For a loyal servant to emerge, a true Son of God must appear on this earth. The archangel must fulfill the duty of a loyal servant by serving that Son of God. The standard of loyalty is determined by loving the Son of God. Therefore, in this historical end time, a son whom God can love must emerge. Only then can the loyal servant be determined.

God called and established John the Baptist to take the place of the archangel who had opposed God for 4,000 years, to replace the archangel who betrayed God, and to pledge loyalty to God. It was to serve Jesus and to empathize with Jesus' difficulties and to exert all efforts to overcome them. However, John the Baptist failed to fulfill that responsibility. The many crowds that welcomed John should have become the crowd that welcomed Jesus. Therefore, John the Baptist was to appear as the representative being of the angelic world, loyal to the true sons and daughters of God, leading the angelic world and defending against the satanic world. Thus, the principle of being a servant was established. "I have come not to be served, but to serve." Where is there a way for the Son of God to do that? It was not something a bridegroom could do. Jesus appealed to the nation from the position of Abel, but there was no Cain among that nation. There was no Cain who had been managed. So, placing the three disciples in the Garden of Gethsemane, Jesus said, "Whether I die or live, let us become one. The three disciples in the Garden of Gethsemane represented the three eras of past, present, and future. They symbolized Cain, Abel, and Seth of Adam's family, Shem, Ham, and Japheth of Noah's family, and the God of Abraham, the God of Isaac, and the God of Jacob, as well as King Saul, King David, and King Solomon. They also symbolized the first Adam, the second Adam, and the third Adam.

These three disciples were to absolutely serve Jesus in the Garden of Gethsemane, which compressed the historical period horizontally, and they were to fulfill the mission of heavenly loyal subjects who would crush Satan when he attacked. Nevertheless, they could not prepare a heart-based foundation to take the blows for Jesus before he was struck, and even while Jesus prayed three times before God, they dozed off.

Thus, Jesus commanded, "The hour of darkness has come; go where you will." This indicates that Jesus was subjected to the historical invasion of Satan.

Thus, Children's Day will emerge. Originally, one must have the justification of children to participate in this feast. Many paths of suffering have been walked to bring this day forth.
