We must be grateful for the days of Parents' Day, Children's Day, and All Things Day. The day of judgment for all days is this day. 
Just as the earth was created and humanity was formed, the holy land can emerge to carry out the providence of finding new children. 

Homeland
<Summary of the Message> The world we live in is certainly not the ideal world we desire. Even when we look at ourselves, our body and mind are not united, and we are not moving toward a single direction and purpose; instead, we are rebelling and fighting. This is not just our situation; the whole world is like this. The past was like this, the present is like this, and the future will also be like this. In such a situation, it is impossible for us to be happy. Everything is contradictory and conflicting. What is the reason for this? It is because, in Christian terms, we have fallen. 
The Purpose of God's Providence
Our body and mind are not united, and tribes, nations, and all of humanity cannot live peacefully within a single ideological realm. While we face this world we do not want and fight through history, we have developed to some extent. However, the fallen world is a world we do not want, a world of sin, and unless we settle this at some point and establish a world where individuals, families, tribes, nations, and the world can sing of peace, freedom, and happiness, we cannot move forward. 
On October 30, 1965, in the afternoon at Daegu Church. 
* This message was given after completing a world tour and visiting the North Gyeongsang Province headquarters during a national tour, and it has been compiled from what was published in <Seonghwa> No. 3 (March 31, 1966). 
God also does not want this fallen world. Therefore, God has come out with a providence of salvation to turn individuals, families, tribes, nations, the world, and the universe back to a God-centered world throughout the past and present. 
Where is the world that is the object of salvation? It is this earth. This earth is a land of sin, and therefore God does not recognize it. Since it does not have the ideals, purposes, and direction that God aims for, it must be settled and undergo a great judgment. That is why a great judgment was carried out in the time of Noah. However, due to Ham's mistake, it has been prolonged, and we must understand that we have not yet escaped the realm of death. Therefore, true individuals, families, nations, the world, and the heavenly kingdom have not yet appeared in this world. This world is placed in a cursed realm that God does not want, which is bound to be under a non-principled authority. Therefore, God sends prophets to take conscientious people from the world of Satan and establish conditions that are unrelated to Satan, allowing them to cross borders and be raised as the chosen people. 
Until the judgment of the end, God works behind history in ways that humans do not know. 
The Mission of the Returning Lord
In order to settle the fallen world, the Messiah will come to this earth as the judge, the representative of sovereignty, and the King of Kings. He must restore the fallen individuals and establish true individual, familial, and national standards. This is because Satan has a national standard to oppose heaven, so he must also establish the sovereignty of heaven. In other words, there must be sovereignty of true individuals, families, tribes, nations, and the world on the side of heaven. God has long ago established the chosen people of Israel and promised the establishment of the territory of Israel.
You have come to hope that Jesus, the Messiah, would be made a king and conquer numerous nations. This is what God desires. There must be a nation, people, tribes, families, and individuals centered on Jesus, but like Jacob, who walked the path of the model example, they must first undergo trials and hardships to be prepared. In other words, it must be achieved under the condition that the whole is opposed and the entire nation and ethnicity are hated. It is from a position that is one hundred percent opposed in the human world that Noah, who obeyed, was welcomed. What is the purpose of this? It is to judge all at once. Noah established a steadfast faith even in a position of persecution, creating a standard for God to judge. Therefore, based on Noah's faith, the judgment was executed at once. It is only right that humanity, which opposed God's will, should be judged all at once.

Historically, you must understand that your ancestors were not blessed on the spot. God commanded Abraham to leave Ur of the Chaldeans for Canaan. When Abraham left his hometown and relatives, if that path was a path of despair, it was indeed a path of despair; if it was a path of discouragement, it was a path of discouragement. However, Abraham, who believed in the promised God, received blessings.

The same was true for Moses. He was not satisfied with life in the palace but thought of the misery of the Israelite people and God, killed the soldiers of Pharaoh, and fled the palace. In the lonely and desolate life in the wilderness, he thought of the sheep as the people of Israel, loved those sheep, and prayed to God for the salvation of the Israelite people. The ancestors, in such times, established hopes for a new providence while suffering and being rejected.

Jesus was also the same. In a position where the entire nation and denomination opposed him, he took on a heavenly responsibility and suffered, establishing a standard of unwavering faith to begin forming the Second Israel. To take back from the evil world, one must first be beaten and then take back. This is the heavenly principle. The ancestors had the conviction that God had already promised them.

What is the homeland of Jesus, the homeland of Moses, the homeland of Jacob, the homeland of Abraham? Where is the homeland that God desires? God laments that He does not have sovereignty to rule over the people and that nation. When God's sovereignty is established, the unification of the world will be achieved at once.

The long history of 6,000 years is a history to restore heavenly sovereignty. Because Jesus could not complete his mission, the world has developed centered on the Christian cultural sphere after Jesus. The desired nation is not America. America is a nation in the preparatory stage. Therefore, America must also be settled. Before a central nation emerges, the nation, tribes, families, and individuals must come forth first. That is why God first seeks individuals.

When Adam fell, he lost the hopeful Adam family, tribe, nation, world, and even God. Jesus came to the altar that had been prepared for 4,000 years to find these, but the altar and the nation and the people opposed him, and he carried the cross. Therefore, the time for Jesus to come again and establish that standard has come to an end. He comes with national, state, and global hopes. That is why Christians are eagerly awaiting the Lord's return, saying, "Come, O Bridegroom!" The true individual, the exemplary male being since the beginning of creation, is the returning Lord.

The mission of this person is to establish a family foundation after achieving personal standards, and to organize tribes, nations, and states. Today, Christian believers hope for the Lamb's Feast, but this feast is not one that is held after being taken up into the air. Since Adam and Eve fell and lost the family standard, the Lamb's Feast is to establish a family by finding the completed Eve, who was completed by the representative Adam. Salvation opens through the pains of childbirth. Since they were born through the blood of fallen parents, the wild olive tree must be cut and grafted onto the true olive tree to bear the true fruit that God can govern.

What is heaven? It is often said to be a paradise or heaven, but it is not a place one goes alone. Heaven is where one's parents and siblings must all go together. To establish heaven, there must be a nation. In other words, there must be a homeland. That is why God is coming to find the day of national liberation.

Jesus also came to establish that homeland, and the prophets and ancestors were the laborers of that homeland's construction. A completed male must come to establish heaven. A man recognized by heaven and earth must establish a family, bear children, and form tribes, nations, and states. Based on Cain and Abel, we must indemnify and graft to establish this world as a homeland under God's dominion. The prophets and ancestors hoped for this, but since they could not build the earthly paradise that connects to the hoped-for individuals, families, tribes, nations, and the world, we must abandon the path we have been on.

To do so, we must walk the path that the world denies and go in the opposite direction of the world, making sacrifices and serving. We must also fast. Now is the end time centered on the Christian cultural sphere, so we must organize a new Israelite nation. This is the mission of religion. However, since Christians are only hoping for their own salvation, that cannot be. God looks at individuals, families, tribes, nations, and states, so the direction and purpose of God's providence is to mobilize religious authority to build heaven.

Where is the true family? It is where there is a true couple and true children. That is why we must establish the chosen people, Israel.

What do we mean by family? It refers to those who can inherit the heart of their parents and rejoice together when God rejoices after establishing a bond of brotherhood. However, until today, there has been no such family of God. Jesus had disciples, but he had no family.

Just as Jacob's twelve sons stopped fighting and loved one another, we too must serve one parent and love one another, and seek out the 72 tribes and relatives. The reason God found me and saved me is not just for me alone, but to establish a greater homeland. We must become the core unit of this family, tribe, and nation.

If humanity had not originally fallen, they would have lived centered on God, but since they could not, they must break away from the world and seek God's embrace. Do you have the heart for national liberation in your hearts?

For an individual to rest, there must be a family foundation, and for a family to rest, the tribal cross must be indemnified. Therefore, by establishing a place of peace on that foundation, one can rest. Thus, to rest, one must manage a larger environment and endure hardships.

To go to heaven, we must unite body and mind, become offerings for the Lord through our families, and build altars. We must lay the pioneering foundation for the door of heaven to open. Before entering heaven, families and tribes must become the people of heaven to finally become the unchanging people of heaven.

Moses was to unite with the nation, but because he could not, God could not allow him to enter Canaan. One must think of the nation and state before thinking of oneself. Tribes, families, and individuals are all within the nation and state. If only the nation and state are established, everything will be complete. Jesus' mission was to prepare a family foundation to welcome the bride.

Homeland Construction
If the Israelite nation had been elevated from the position of being a servant to a son, and from the position of a son to a direct child centered on Jesus, they would have conquered Rome within 40 years. However, Jesus was crucified, and he has come to reorganize Israel with a standard of hope in the spirit world. Therefore, everyone must wait for the Second Coming with a faith of unity, but since they are divided, they all perish.

The mission of the Unification Church is to engrave my homeland in my heart and fulfill the duty of a loyal subject, asking how to organize the homeland. Before God meets the day of glory, even Jesus must pray in the spirit world.

Where is the homeland? It is neither America nor Korea. There must be a homeland where the organization of families, tribes, and nations has been achieved, regardless of the place. For 6,000 years, God has walked over many nations while hoping for the heavenly kingdom to be established on this earth. He has come looking for the loyal and virtuous ones of heaven, so now we must reorganize the nation, people, and families centered on heaven.

We must not forget that we have been called for the day of liberation for national liberation. The construction of the homeland is the mission of religious people, yet there are those who harbor the wicked desire to seek only their own salvation.

We boast of Parents' Day, Children's Day, and the Day of All Things, but there is no Day of God. God must be able to move freely, but He cannot do so. Jesus also came to establish a nation. Without a homeland, it is pitiful. Because there is no homeland, religious people have been miserable. To judge, individuals, families, tribes, nations, and the world must stand on an unchanging standard, and based on that standard, judgment will be made. The homeland is the ultimate hope. The homeland includes the nation, tribe, family, and individual.

Has this three thousand li become the homeland? Since it has not, it must be settled. We must all work wholeheartedly to establish the homeland that God desires, that Jesus desires, that the Holy Spirit desires, and that the prophets and ancestors desire. If we do not, we cannot stand before God.

The good things and joys of today must be used as strength for tomorrow. For the sake of the will, the teacher has given up everything. It was only for the will.

God, do you know... Can you all pray like this?

To establish the Abel altar, we must build a national altar. We must also recognize Cain's altar. In the past, Cain killed Abel, but in the end times, they must cooperate. We must build an Abel-like national altar. By doing so, we can subdue Cain. We must establish unchanging principles while building personal, family, tribal, and national altars. That is how it can be done.

Gyeongbuk is the center of faith. We must make significant contributions centered on Gyeongbuk. Then, the world will revive centered on this nation.

Heart connects with everyone
Spiritual phenomena are bound to occur in the current society.

It is difficult to walk the path of purpose for more than seven years for heaven. Jacob's 21 years of hardship is commendable. The question is whether one lives for God, for humanity, or for oneself.

Up until today, humanity has lived entangled in problems that must be solved by humans themselves. They have not engaged with the cosmic problems that must be resolved with God.

Where am I? Am I at a standstill or making progress? If I am at a standstill, what am I doing it for? The father that the teacher calls "Father!" and the father that you call "Father!" have different meanings.

Until today, we have come out with a superficial view of faith. We have lost our subjectivity. The Unification Church is said to have many conditions. These conditions are not for God, the teacher, or the church, but for you. It is because you have not been pure that the condition of one-on-one is necessary.

To fulfill the purpose, the whole must start at once, but since that cannot happen, we must carry the historical conditions. Because we only go with hope, we stumble. Heaven cannot punish those who suffer more. Rather, the spirit world mobilizes to assist in the swift realization of the purpose. One must have relativity and be able to rejoice in the subject.

Truth governs the world.

Let us become true family members
Most people live in the place where they were born or where their parents and siblings live. While living there, one may be happy on one hand and unhappy on the other.

When looking at a household, no matter how happy a person may be, they do not only need a house. They need not only their own house but also a neighborhood where that house can be established, and they need a neighborhood, a town or county, and further, a country. Is that not so? Moreover, a world where that country can exist is necessary, and that world requires a greater heaven and earth.

The original family that God desires
Until now, countless humans have been born, lived, and died. They were born in one house, became parents of one family, gave birth to children, formed one family, and lived for their country or for something else before going to the spirit world. Many people still live like this on this earth. Among the countless people who have come and gone, if there was someone who lived from a good position, they are infinitely happy.

If one is human, deep in their heart, they are always searching for something more perfect, more precious, more ideal, and more valuable. Looking at this, are the country, society, family, parents, siblings, and even oneself that we live in today perfect? How is it? Is it perfect? Is it not perfect? Humans always hope for something better, more precious, and more peaceful.

In this world, we live in a position where I cannot guarantee myself forever, nor can my family guarantee me forever, and my parents cannot guarantee me forever. The country cannot guarantee me either, nor can any ideology in the world. Therefore, we humans wish for one being who can guarantee us from our individual selves to our families, societies, nations, and the entire world, that is, an absolute subject of happiness, an eternal subject of ideals, and an absolute subject of goodness. This is the hope of many humans today.

Is the house we live in today a true home? In your birthplace, there are parents who provide you with clothing when it is cold, food when you are hungry, and a path to learning when you are ignorant. There will be siblings around you who help with everything. Are you, born as a son or daughter in a family with such parents and siblings, truly happy? It is said that you are not happy. For some reason, you are always searching for something more complete and more precious. Those who cannot find a place where they can sing happiness with truly loving parents and can praise that "this is my eternal welfare" in the embrace of siblings are unhappy. That is why many young people today are leaving their families.

Parents wish for their children to be devoted sons and daughters, and nations wish for their citizens to be loyal subjects and virtuous women. Originally, the path of devoted sons and daughters and the path of loyal subjects and virtuous women is the path of life, but why are humans unable to walk that path? It is because our original hearts do not align with our lives and social environments and are in conflicting positions. There is always a desire in one part of the heart to seek a new nation, a new world, and something new, which leads to the movement of the heart to deny reality and rush toward a new world. We cannot deny this.

Today, when you look at yourself or your family, you cannot deny that you are living while hoping for something better without even realizing it. If this imperfect state continues forever, the history that started from imperfection will conclude in imperfection, so every human, without exception, desires to escape from an evil environment based on a conscience that aims for goodness and a nature that seeks to connect with the heavenly principles. This is an undeniable fact that arises because there is a true heart facing the heavenly principles.

Therefore, if we speak of such a world using religious terminology, we call it a fallen world.

Some people are looking toward the original family, but they do not know how to establish the original family or how to have original siblings and original parents.

The love of parents and siblings who love me is a love that can be welcomed anywhere in the world. Since I do not have the original family, original parents, and original siblings that I can have, being born and living among the current parents and siblings means I am not my original self. That is why we are at a crossroads of denying our current selves and starting from our original selves, stumbling in our lives today.

Since the day humanity's ancestors fell, countless historical paths have passed, but the original family, original siblings, and original parents have not yet appeared on this earth. Therefore, God has been working to find the original family, original siblings, and original parents to connect them to the original nation and the original world, which has been God's providential history until now.

Today, we hope for a family other than the one we live in, which is in a non-principled world. That hoped-for family is also desired by God, so God is coming down to find that hoped-for family, and we humans are unknowingly going up to find that hoped-for family. In other words, God is coming to introduce the original family, and humans are going to find the original family without even realizing it. Do you understand?

However, can this original family appear all at once? It cannot. For a true family to emerge in this fallen land, what stages must be gone through? Before the original sons and daughters come forth, the original servants must come out, and then the original adopted children must come forth. After that, the original sons and daughters will emerge.
In a fallen world, we humans, no matter how loyal we are or how capable we may seem, are beings that cannot even become servants before God, who created heaven and earth. Have you ever tried to be a servant of God? If you don't even know whether God exists or not, how can you become a servant of God? We were in a past where we could not even aspire to be God's servants. Only after passing through the position of a servant and the position of an adopted child can we become direct children. After going through such stages, we can finally meet God as our parent. This is what we call the history of restoration. The history of restoration.

To build the original family that was lost, many people today refer to this time, when God has been working for 6,000 years, as the last days. So what is this end time referred to as the last days? In this world, there are groups that are like original servants, groups that are like original adopted children, and groups that are like original children. The time when the original parents come upon the group that is like the original children is called the end time. This is the thought of the Second Coming. Therefore, Jesus said, "I am the bridegroom, and you are the bride." It means that a father and mother must appear on earth.

The wedding feast of the Lamb is when the original family, which humanity has lost, is established on this planet. So what is needed to build that original family? There must be parents, there must be siblings, and there must be servants. Only on such a foundation can children multiply, and only then can the original lineage be formed, the original nation be established, and the original world be realized. Thus, we know well that the history of restoration has been carried out to burn away this wicked world and to establish the original world of creation.

Today, in our Unification Church, we refer to our members as family. No one has enlightened us on the term "family" in the historical course up to now. The term "family" cannot exist apart from a home. For a family to arise, there must be a home, and for that home to exist, there must be siblings, and for siblings to exist, there must be parents. Is that not so? "Yes." In Christianity, while terms like members or believers have been used, the term "family" has not been used. Today, while the world is clamoring for a global extended family in an external sense, to form such an extended family, there must be parents who can be a father and mother of that extended family. The one who comes as those parents is the Messiah. Do you understand? "Yes."

However, among those referred to as family in today's Unification Church, there are true family members and those who are the opposite. There are also family members in a middle position. Then, who are the true family members who possess the term "family" centered on the heavenly family established by God? This is the question.

To become a family member, one must first have parents. To be siblings, there must also be parents. While there may be many siblings, there is only one parent, which is the principle. Therefore, family members living a life of faith will inevitably long for their relative family members when walking the path of the cross, encountering sorrow and loneliness, or facing tribulations. Rather than being sad alone, when one goes to find family members and shares their circumstances, they should encourage each other, saying, "Let us surely overcome our enemies." They must support and comfort each other and be a source of strength for one another. Those who cannot stand in this position are not true family members, nor are they true brothers.

Those on the front lines fighting bear the direct burden of the cross. Therefore, those in the rear should not complain, even if they cannot take on their cross. In the coming days, there is a preparation for us, so if the younger brother says, "I will go," or if the elder brother says, "I will go," how wonderful it would be to have encouragement backing them up! If, when Jesus was crucified, his beloved three disciples had also been crucified alongside him, saying, "Lord! Please relieve your injustice. We will surely resolve your grievances for our descendants," how much strength would that have given Jesus! If that had happened, Jesus would not have prayed at the moment of his death, "My God, why have you forsaken me?" but rather, "Father, please establish us and resolve the grievances of this world, and forgive them!" 

If that had happened, the history of Christianity would not have extended to two thousand years. Jesus represented his beloved disciples before God, saying, "These have borne all the crosses on behalf of all humanity, and they have also given me strength on my path to death, serving me without regard for their own deaths." Is not the person God seeks such sons and daughters? It should have been so, but Jesus felt sorrow for not being able to fulfill that.

Today, our unified family is walking a difficult path. Our church is finally calling each other family. We are using the nouns brother and child. Though heaven and earth may pass away, this holy noun must not disappear. Even if history is judged and this era is judged and disappears, these nouns and realities must remain. Even if this world is cleared away, the hopeful family, the hopeful home, and the hopeful brothers must remain. This is God's ideal. For these hopeful families to remain completely, they must overcome the historical path of the cross.

Today, before us lie not only individual crosses but also family, tribal, national, global, and even cosmic crosses. God sent Jesus as the Messiah to the Jewish nation after four thousand years to restore that nation and people and to return the world to a heavenly sovereign nation centered around that people.

Today, the mission to restore that sovereign nation must be accomplished through the Republic of Korea, which is currently quite chaotic. Therefore, when the elder brother walks the path of death, the younger brother must follow. If the younger brother wishes to go, the elder brother must follow. If the parents go, the children must go, and if the children go, the parents must go. We must take on common responsibility and lead one family, one tribe, one nation, one world, and ultimately one cosmos. Therefore, we must recognize that we have the mission to advance through greater crosses at each stage of the restoration path. You all stand in such a position.

The complete way of life as a young person in the Unification Church
Now my heart knows God's will, and my body and emotions wish to experience God's heart. What I desire is to create a peaceful family, peaceful family members, and peaceful brothers who can sing of freedom and liberation on the foundation of happiness. Who can take away this longing heart?

Centered on my Father, God, and centered on the True Parents, we can form one family, one nation, and one world. When this central God and True Parents are pleased, joy will overflow from there, filling heaven and earth, and our desire for this will never be forgotten, even if we must die a hundred or a thousand times. This is the duty to be resolved in life, the greatest path of the cross that fallen humanity must walk, and we must not stumble on the small path of the cross.

Even while you sleep, there are elder brothers or sisters, younger siblings, or family members shedding tears and praying. You must also be aware that there are hungry family members when you are full. So, whether you eat or sleep, you must pray with a tearful heart to give them spiritual strength.

You should create an altar and always keep it clean, appealing to be a sacrifice that can be offered before God, day or night. If you cannot bear the responsibility of action or reality, you must at least make that inner preparation and become one who fights with tears.

In the path of tribulation, you must cling to the connections of family members carrying the cross; otherwise, you will soon be separated from those who are fighting alongside you. If that happens, you will become a laggard and a defeated soldier.

What is the complete way of life as a young person in the Unification Church? It is to break through the raging storms on the front lines and to advance through all paths of the cross with determination. This is the way of the heart that God desires. Those who have not felt sorrow in such a position will not understand through explanation. When one cries out, "Father!" in such a position, they will come to know the labor of the Father who bore the historical cross and realize that not being a true filial child before the Father is God's sorrow. 

God's desire was to meet true filial sons and daughters in such a position, and when one says, "Oh! Thank you, so-and-so," that is when the position of filial sons and daughters, loyal subjects, and virtuous women is determined.

We must not be in comfortable positions. Therefore, whether we farm or do anything else, we must take hold of the hoe and overturn the land of three thousand li, digging up the world. We must stand in a position to cross the hill of the cross together as brothers, both emotionally and circumstantially.

We must create the true children, true families, and true family members that God has longed for and desired until now. Who must do this? Humans must do it. If God had done it alone, it would not have taken six thousand years. It has always been extended because humans have failed to take responsibility.

Today, the Korean people have no attachment or interest in anything. In such times, what should our Unification Church do? After going through three-year and seven-year courses, when we enter the rural areas, we must take up the hoe, love the farmland with farmers, and cultivate the land with true hearts, shedding tears.

We must teach the children whom parents have failed to educate, awaken those who have been indifferent to education, and rekindle interest and attachment in this nation, which has returned to an individualistic stance and lost its interest and attachment to the country.

However, when we enter the village, we will find ourselves in a position of opposition. It may seem unjust and frustrating at first, but it is the best position to raise interest and create issues. Even if they unite to oppose, we must push through and deliver the message and serve. Before they judge right and wrong, they think it is bad unconditionally, and they all unite to insult and mistreat us in their own way. However, as time passes, they will realize, "I did not shed tears for this land, but they are shedding tears. I did not teach the children, but they are teaching our children. I, as a local leader, did not shed tears or take action for this nation and people, but they are doing that work. I opposed and persecuted unconditionally, but now I see that they shed tears for this nation, sweat for this land, and endure the path of suffering and hunger for our children. What have I done?"

When we think of such things, we realize that it was good to be insulted. Even if there is opposition, when the whole community opposes, it raises interest, and later, they will feel that they were wrong. (The following words were not recorded.)

The path of restoration we must return to
The title I want to speak to you about today is "The Path of Restoration We Must Return To."

Those who have just come may not understand the meaning of the term "restoration" as mentioned in the Unification Church. The term restoration means to return to the original position. Humanity has become a world of evil due to the fall, so it means that we who live in this world of evil must return to the original world of goodness that has not fallen. In other words, it means returning to the world before the fall.

Thus, we have a path of restoration that we must walk.

Creation and Fall of Humanity
God, who created heaven and earth, created humanity as beings He loves dearly. Among the creations made over six days, He created humanity with a heartfelt desire to establish them as the object of His glory and hope.

We must once again reflect on how much God has longed for that one human being to grow, fulfill His hope, and create a peaceful family where they can live together in happiness.

God was pleased to create the original Adam and Eve, but due to the fall, He has been filled with a sorrowful and earnest heart, longing for the time when He could complete a victory. We must think about this again. It was good to look at the created world prepared for Adam and Eve, but it was even better to see the growing Adam and Eve who would govern all things; this was the heart of the Father that we must understand.

Adam and Eve were to be the foundation of hope and happiness before God, and they were to be the central beings in the universe, without whom nothing could exist. Therefore, they should not have fallen, nor should there have been a day of sorrow. However, due to one day's mistake, the term "fall" was attached, leading to the emergence of the term "sorrow," and the powers of darkness appeared in the world that God hoped for. We must recognize that this fact is both unjust and tragic.

It is natural for humanity to suffer due to the fall of the ancestors of humanity, but we must realize how tragic it is that God, who looked upon those ancestors with a heart of hope, has also had to suffer because of them. Because humanity fell into a place of sorrow, God had to stand in a position of injustice and pain. Such events that should not have happened in heaven and earth, or that could not even be imagined, occurred due to the mistakes of the ancestors of humanity, which we must recognize as the fall of humanity.

Did Adam and Eve fall knowing all of God's heart and the purpose of creation? No, they did not. If Adam and Eve had fallen from a position of completeness, having realized everything, then God's creation ideology and work could not have been completed. Therefore, Adam and Eve did not fall from a position where they knew all of God's content and could govern everything as valuable beings who inherited the entirety of God's purpose; rather, they fell during their growth process when they did not know everything.

Today, many in established churches believe that Adam and Eve fell as a man and woman who had become adults, knowing all the principles of heaven and earth and having the authority to inherit God's heart and creation work.

However, Adam and Eve fell from a position where they did not know such content. They did not fall from a position of completion but from a position where they were hoping for completion. If they had fallen from a position of completion, we could say that there is a possibility of falling even in the completed world, which we call heaven. Therefore, we can understand that Adam and Eve fell at an incomplete stage.

Adam and Eve could not hold God's creation work and ideals in their hearts and could not live in a single-minded devotion to truly love God, and they fell. Thus, the world formed is the world where fallen descendants live today, and we must recognize that this is what has made the world evil. Therefore, we must understand that the hope God had when He created Adam and Eve remains as hope. The loss of a person who could fulfill that hope is God's sorrow.

The greater that hope is, the greater God's sorrow becomes in proportion to that hope, and the more intense God's hope is, the more significant internal suffering God experiences. We cannot deny this.

Until now, ordinary believers have not known that God is a sorrowful being, and humanity has been created.
I did not truly understand that God was the one who sighed. Until today, I did not realize that the Creator, who made heaven and earth, was placed in a position of sorrow due to human mistakes.  
The Kingdom of Hope  
For whom was heaven created? Heaven was not created for God Himself, but for humanity. Therefore, the owner of heaven is not God, but humanity. The ideal of heaven was established centered on humanity, but because humanity has fallen apart, the ideal of heaven has remained as an ideal, and heaven has become a heaven without content, leaving only the noun "heaven," which means that God has been unable to sing of satisfaction, joy, and happiness. In other words, God has not been able to be the God of glory. Heaven has been empty and submerged in sorrow until now. Due to the fallen Adam, this earth has entered into the realm of Satan, and we must understand that the power of Satan has pushed open the gates of heaven and swept up to the throne of God. Therefore, what has God hoped for until now? If God has hope for the fallen human world, it is about how to restore the original hope of Adam and Eve before the fall. You must understand that God has been coming forth until now, looking forward to that day of restoration.  
What is salvation? To save someone who has fallen into water means to restore them to their state before they fell into the water, and to save someone who is sick means to restore them to their state before they became ill.  
So, what must Jesus do when He comes again today? He must become the Savior. After becoming the Savior, He can also be a brother, an elder brother, and anything else we desire. If this world had not fallen and had become the original world that God desired, there would be no need for Jesus as the Savior, but because this earth is still groaning in the world of sin, a Savior is needed. Therefore, the world where Jesus can be welcomed not as a Savior but as a brother or elder brother is the heaven we hope for.  
What kind of world does the Lord who is coming again want to establish? It is the original world before the fall, the world that God pursued and desired within His ideals, a world where He can achieve the meaning of completion and embrace the whole world with joy. The only begotten Son of the loving God, Adam and Eve, who were born as princes and princesses, have fallen apart due to the fall, so we must reclaim this position.  
We must reclaim it while saying, "Heaven and earth are mine." Everyone desires to make this world their own, and that is the original desire. How wonderful it is! Who is God? He is my Father. There is no need to explain who God is. We can naturally know God from birth.  
God, who has lost the kingdom of hope, has been working hard until today to find the kingdom of hope for humanity, and you will know that humanity has sought the kingdom of hope through a long historical journey.  
Then, if there is something that God longs for in His heart, what could it be? In the process of establishing the kingdom of hope, what does God desire most? The people living on this earth have all become dead children due to the fall, and because they have inherited the sinful lineage of Satan, there are no direct descendants whom God can love and hold onto. Therefore, God has been working in providence to restore humanity born of Satan's lineage. To what extent must restoration occur? It must be restored to the position of direct sons and daughters. However, humanity has fallen to the position of the lowest servants due to the fall. What is the lowest servant? The lowest servant cannot have a master. A servant has a master, but the lowest servant does not have a master. Therefore, God is taking the lowest servants who are in the position of servants from the realm of Satan to save them. He is taking the lowest servants belonging to Satan, making them pledge loyalty before God, and restoring them as the lowest servants on heaven's side.  
God's providence of salvation and central figures  
What kind of era was the Old Testament age? It was the age of servants. It was the era of restoring humans in the position of the lowest servants to the position of servants. Therefore, Abraham was a servant and could not be a son. God established the lowest servant to fulfill the duty of loyalty. Thus, He gathered the historical world of humanity and developed God's providence while occupying the global stage of evil on heaven's side. Jacob also did not win as a son of God but won from the position of a servant. God has been working in providence to restore from the lowest servant to the position of a servant, and from the position of a servant to the position of a son.  
The New Testament age was the era of restoring servants to sons. Romans 8:23 states that even we, who have received the first fruits of the Spirit, groan inwardly, waiting for our adoption as sons. This means that we desire to be adopted before God.  
Adopted children have a different lineage. Therefore, after establishing the position of adopted children, the direct sons and daughters of God must come and, like grafting a wild olive shoot onto a cultivated olive tree, they must liberate the relationship of adopted children and establish the relationship of direct children. This was the hope that Jesus had to fulfill without dying.  
To restore from the lowest servant to a servant, from a servant to an adopted child, and from an adopted child to direct sons and daughters, what must be done? Originally, God's creation ideal is to complete the kingdom of heaven on earth while simultaneously completing the kingdom of heaven in heaven, establishing God's emotional foundation on this earth and paving the way to heaven. Only then can one become the original, non-fallen sons and daughters. However, because Jesus came to this earth and could not teach the ideals of the kingdom of heaven on earth and the kingdom of heaven in heaven, and only accomplished spiritual salvation, Jesus became the only begotten Son praying to God from the position of an adopted child. The fact that He is praying indicates that Jesus did not fulfill His purpose completely.  
What have Jesus and the Holy Spirit been doing for 2,000 years? They have been praying before God and seeking the day of hope, paving the way from the earth to heaven. So, where did Jesus go after He died? He went to paradise. What is paradise? It is the waiting room to enter heaven. But why does the only begotten Son of God, Jesus, pray before God? It is because He did not complete His responsibility. Originally, Jesus was to come as the True Parents of all humanity. However, because He could not establish the relationship of True Parents with all humanity, He must return to the earth. It is not a heavenly return but an earthly return that must happen.  
Jesus, who came looking at the kingdom of heaven, had to place the Israelite people in the position of servants and establish the principles of adopted children and the position of direct children to unite with Jesus. Thus, He intended to bless the Israelite people from God so that the sons and daughters born from them could be placed in a position where they could say they have nothing to do with the fallen world, but Jesus could not accomplish that and returned. Therefore, God has been looking toward the kingdom of restoration until now. If God has hope, what is it? It is the original Adam and Eve, whom He created with all His hopes and desires, pouring out His heart and soul. However, because they fell, who did He send as a substitute? Jesus.  
Jesus is the one who came as the second Adam to replace the original Adam. He came as the restored Adam without relation to the fall. Jesus is the second Adam, and the Lord who is coming again will come as the third Adam.  
So, what must He do when He comes? He must establish the kingdom of hope. He must establish the kingdom of heaven on earth and the kingdom of heaven in heaven. If we analyze the overall content of God's providence throughout history, we can understand that God has been seeking the original Adam and Eve who did not fall on the path of restoration. Because humans have inherited the lineage of Satan due to the fall, they cannot become God's people without passing through God's lineage. Even though these wicked descendants exist, God still hopes that these humans will believe in Jesus and rise to the position before the fall, and He has come forth with hope for tomorrow. However, how many people have believed in Jesus and risen to the position of Adam and Eve before the fall until today? Not a single person.  
Jesus and the True Parents  
Through 4,000 years of effort, God finally established Jesus, the hope of the restored Adam-type who did not fall. So, who is Jesus before the people of this earth? He is the True Ancestor. If the human ancestors, Adam and Eve, had not fallen and had fulfilled God's will, they would have become the True Ancestors of humanity, but due to the fall, Adam and Eve lost the position of the True Ancestor of humanity that God wanted to establish as the ideal of creation.  
No matter how capable or powerful a person may be, every human is born with the fallen lineage of their ancestors. This is a regrettable fact. Humanity, with fallen ancestors, is rushing toward hell, and throughout history, they have sought to establish a standard and find the original parents who can embrace the True Children. Therefore, what has God sought through 4,000 years of restoration? He has sought to find the original position that Adam and Eve lost.  
So, what is the Messiah? The Messiah must first become the Savior from the position of True Parents, as humanity has lost the position of True Parents due to the fall.  
What is the Feast of the Lamb? Originally, God said to Adam and Eve, "You are the chosen ones, the direct sons and daughters of the Lord of heaven and earth, and I am glad that my bloodline has emerged on this earth because of you," and this refers to receiving the blessing of inheriting all of God's great legacy and the blessing of marriage. Thus, the one who was to represent God's full authority was Adam and Eve before the fall, but because they fell, all of God's creation ideals were shattered.  
6,000 years ago, it was necessary to establish the kingdom of hope centered on them, but due to the fall, it was shattered into pieces.  
Therefore, to restore humanity from the lowest servant to a servant, from a servant to an adopted child, and from an adopted child to direct sons and daughters, it is to subdue Satan and receive the blessing of marriage from God as the victorious prince, which is the Feast of the Lamb. Christianity does not understand this content well. If you do not believe this fact, please pray. The day when humanity completes the salvation of the lost True Parents due to the fall and restores them is the Feast of the Lamb. This day must come for everything to be fulfilled.  
Good humans are only born under good parents. And from there, a proper family is formed, and only when a proper family is established can a proper lineage, nation, and world be formed. This is the process of restoration.  
What was in God's hope before Adam and Eve fell? It was to establish a lineage centered on the original True Parents, forming tribes, nations, and the world. Thus, the original ideal of God's creation was to establish the kingdom of heaven, but due to the fall of humanity, parents fell apart and children fell apart, leading to the world we see today.  
So, how will the Lord who is coming in the future come? Matthew 24 records that He will come in the glory of the Father. The first Adam fell, and the second Adam did not fulfill His will on earth, so the returning Lord will come as the third Adam in their place. Because the 3 billion people living on this earth have not passed through the lineage of True Parents, they cannot establish a relationship with God in this current state. Therefore, the one who comes with the relationship of True Parents is the returning Lord. So, what has the 6,000 years of history been? It has been the history of restoring the completed standard of the lost True Parents, namely Adam and Eve.  
What is the path of restoration? Originally, there should be no need for the noun "Savior." We should be able to welcome the Lord as a brother with whom we can consult, becoming citizens of heaven and ancestors of restoration. Shouldn't that be the case? Then why must we walk the path of restoration? It is because of the fall. If there had been no fall, it would have been settled in one go, but due to the fall, it has to go through three generations. Thus, it has passed through the era of the Old Testament, which is the era of rebirth, and the era of the New Testament, which is the era of growth. And in the future, we must go through the era of the New Covenant, which is the era of completion, based on the example of the Lord who is coming anew. The historical distance that has been traveled to recreate one Adam is the restoration history up to now.  
In the family of Adam, God's will to restore centered on Cain and Abel was pushed out of the family of Adam to the family of Noah because Abel did not fulfill his responsibility. And this has extended from the time of Noah to the time of Abraham, from the time of Abraham to the time of Moses, and from the time of Moses to the time of Jesus. However, Jesus also could not resolve God's deep sorrow, and this will has been extended again through the 2,000 years of history of Jesus and the Holy Spirit up to now. You must understand that this historical flow did not happen by itself but has unfolded according to God's providential program of restoration. You must also understand that God has been groping along this path of restoration.  
Because the standard of restoration was not established in the family of Adam, God spent 1,600 years to establish the family of Noah in place of the family of Adam. When God warned Noah that there would be a flood judgment after 120 years, Noah himself did not know what God's heart was like. All he heard were commands. He did not know the specifics of the content that after 120 years, He would surely judge this world. Noah did not know that God had come to Him with a solemn determination to resolve His internal sadness and sorrow. However, Noah faithfully kept the promise he made with God, with a single-minded faith, never forgetting it.  
So, what was Noah supposed to do for 120 years at that time? To become the ancestor of restoration, in other words, to become the second human ancestor, he had to overcome the harsh winds, severe trials, and harsh environments of that wicked world. No matter what trials he faced, Noah had to stand on a firm foundation of faith, determined not to stand in the position of breaking the heavenly law and betraying God, just like Adam. Therefore, the 120 years Noah spent building the ark on Mount Ararat was not a happy period. As time passed, many people of that era treated Noah as a crazy old man. However, Noah, amidst the mockery, ridicule, and the environment filled with injustice and resentment, did not abandon the promise he made with God and overcame that environment with unwavering faith.  
Noah's eight family members, including his wife and children, also denied Noah. The Bible does not contain this content. Why was that? It was because for 120 years, he was doing only that work; what would his wife and children have said? Imagine being Noah's wife or child. Would you be able to do that? For 120 years, he was doing such things, so what would his appearance have been like? His beloved wife resented Noah, and his beloved children also resented him. Originally, they hoped to believe in him and built that family, hoping to believe in him.
was sent to establish a true individual, but there was none. Was there a true family? There were many families, but no true family. There were no true tribes, true nations, or true countries. In the valley of the Mount of Olives, looking at Jerusalem with a heart full of heavenly hope, Jesus was filled with sorrow to find a true individual.

The disciples of the Messiah, who came to govern heaven and earth, were just fishermen... Two thousand years ago, the fishermen of Israel were considered lowly. How could such people be disciples before the Messiah? This is truly a tragic historical irony. 

Jesus came to fulfill the hope of humanity and to establish the kingdom of heaven on earth, yet he faced rejection and misunderstanding. The very people he came to save turned against him, and the promise of the kingdom remained unfulfilled. 

The history of Israel, marked by suffering and trials, is a testament to the consequences of rejecting the Messiah. The pain of Jesus, who bore the sins of the world, is a reflection of the deep sorrow of God, who desires to see His kingdom established.

As we reflect on this history, we must recognize the importance of fulfilling the mission entrusted to us. The hope of the Messiah is not just a distant promise; it is a call to action for all of us. We must seek to build the kingdom of heaven on earth, starting with ourselves, our families, and our communities.

In this final age, as we await the return of the Messiah, we must understand our role in this divine plan. The kingdom of heaven is not merely a spiritual concept; it requires tangible efforts to establish it in our world. We must strive to embody the values of love, unity, and peace that the Messiah represents.

Let us not forget the lessons of history. The rejection of Jesus led to immense suffering for the people of Israel and the world. We must learn from this and ensure that we do not repeat the mistakes of the past. Instead, let us embrace the hope of the Messiah and work towards the realization of the kingdom of heaven on earth. 

In doing so, we honor the sacrifice of Jesus and fulfill the divine purpose for which he came. The time has come for us to rise up and take responsibility for our role in God's plan. The kingdom of heaven is within our reach, but it requires our commitment and dedication to bring it to fruition.
Before Peter became the chief disciple, what does this mean? Think about it, everyone. 
Where have the well-believed teachers of the law, scribes, and priests gone? Among the 12 disciples, there was not a single one from the teachers of the law, scribes, or priests. Those who were well-believed all betrayed Jesus and boarded the train to hell. Could they have gone to heaven? They became direct disciples of the god Baal, so that was not possible. Nevertheless, the disciples, who were fishermen at the lowest level, were able to go to paradise because they were chosen as Jesus' disciples. 
Is the Lord you believe in the bridegroom? It is a frustrating and resentful matter. Therefore, to resolve the grievances of 2,000 years, Jesus must come again to this earth. To come, a foundation must be laid to resolve those grievances. For this reason, at the end of times, just as the scribes and priests of Jesus' time had to stand in the place of Jesus' apostles, the scholars scattered around the world must first welcome the Lord who is coming, saying, "Oh Lord, come." Thus, history tends to recreate the history of the past. 
If Jesus had come riding with the sound of the archangel's trumpet from the position where the leaders of Judaism, such as teachers of the law and priests, exercised their power, how well would they have received Jesus? The Jewish people only knew that Jesus would come on a cloud. Is it reasonable to say that Jesus worked as a carpenter's assistant? How miserable must have been Jesus' situation, who had to work as a carpenter's assistant? Just hearing about that carpenter makes my insides twist. This is because the people of Israel could not take responsibility. For over 30 years, carrying grievances in his heart and looking forward to a hopeful time, even Jesus' mother, Mary, could not take responsibility. 
At the wedding feast in Cana, Jesus looked at his mother and said, "Woman, what does this have to do with me?" (John 2:4), and when the crowd told Jesus that his mother and brothers were outside wanting to speak to him, Jesus replied, "Who is my mother, and who are my brothers? For whoever does the will of my Father in heaven is my brother and sister and mother." (Matthew 12:50). Today, Christians must understand the heart of Jesus well. 
Do you know at what age Jesus left home, filled with grievances? He was hated by Joseph's direct children, even while working differently from his brothers in Joseph's household. Even during the holidays, he never got to wear new clothes. What position was Jesus in? Although Joseph was raising him under God's command, Jesus was a stepson, so he was disliked. 
Even during the holidays, he could not have a heart to praise God with his father and mother, so in sadness and injustice, Jesus went up to the Jerusalem temple regardless of whether his parents were there or not. Knowing that he had the responsibility to protect the Jerusalem temple, he devoted himself near the temple where the priests stayed. 
Who would have thought that Jesus, who had so many grievances, would suffer so much to fulfill God's will on this earth? What does the cross mean to the Messiah, who came as God's only begotten Son and the savior of all mankind? 
Today, as I take responsibility for the Unification Church, I have faced more persecution than anyone else and have been cursed before this nation. However, let them persecute, trample, and despise the Unification Church, saying it is heretical. The roots are meant to go deeper. Let’s see who is true and who is false. The true will surely win. 
I have heard all kinds of insults, so I could curse the nation and the church, but because I knew the path Jesus walked and understood God's sorrowful heart and the road to restoration, I endured and came out. I am not someone who would easily die just because I am thrown into prison. 
Today, the warriors of unification are walking the remaining path of restoration. The master was born in this Republic of Korea today, but if this master had been born in America, he would not have had to suffer such endless hardships. 
The path of restoration that must be walked again 
When Jesus came to find the Israelite people as the savior and Messiah, who among the Israelites offered him a bowl of rice? Who gave him a piece of clothing? No one did. Who would have known the situation of Jesus, who wanted to eat the fruit of the fig tree upon entering Jerusalem? Knowing the sorrowful and resentful heart of Jesus makes one feel heartbroken. 
So what does it mean to believe in Jesus? It means to become a true disciple among the disciples. Therefore, the warriors of unification must resolve the grievances of Jesus, who had so many grievances, and fulfill the heavenly kingdom that God hoped for. To do this, we must become true people who can go to heaven. After that, we must become true families and true nations. We must look forward to this. 
God has come seeking individuals and families along the path of restoration, but he has been rejected by those individuals and families. That father, who does not stop his steps toward the world again, makes me want to go as well. Should I refuse because the path is rugged? Should I refuse because there is death on that path? Should I refuse because there are sad circumstances? 
Since I must walk the path my father walked, if my father is in difficulty, I should wish to be in difficulty too, and if my father is sad, I should wish to be sad too. This is the ideology of unification. Thus, based on this small peninsula of 3,000 ri, we must create an extraordinary movement before this nation and raise a new whirlwind in the world. We must raise a new banner so that democracy and communism are absorbed within our ideological realm. 
Every time I think of this nation and stand before God, my heart swells. When I realize that this intention is indeed the will established by my father, I must overcome any difficulty. Also, no matter how difficult the circumstances may be, since he is my father and my circumstances, I must inherit the tradition established by that father and be grafted into his history and heart. If that father suffers, I too must suffer. This is the natural principle. Therefore, Christians today must not sleep. They must not rest. Among Christians today, there are many denominations that have sung about a day of rest. However, Unification Church members must not rest and must walk that path. 
Just as Jesus prayed and preached even in the place of death on Mount Calvary, you, Unification Church members, must evangelize even in this world engulfed by the darkness of death. Even if you go to hell, you must evangelize the most pitiful person there. 
The footsteps of the warriors of unification 
Compared to the effort God has made to save us, the tears, blood, and sweat we have shed to raise even one child in one place are nothing. Therefore, we must go on, thinking of how God has led the history of restoration over 6,000 years as a providence of recreation to resolve grievances. 
The love and concern you have for the teacher are good. I appreciate that sincerity. However, I do not want you to love me more than you love this nation and this people. Therefore, you must love this nation as much as you love the teacher. You must become those who shed tears for not being able to give to the nation. It is right to go to the nation, which is in a poor situation, hoping to save its dying life, and serve them. Only then will the teacher's heart be at peace. When you bring porridge for the teacher, if you have that sincerity, then share it for the 30 million people, for all humanity, and for the entire heaven and earth. This is the thought of unification. 
The teacher has starved more than anyone else, has been insulted more than anyone else, and has been beaten more than anyone else. Furthermore, even in the labor field, the teacher is the top worker. Today, Koreans think that just eating well in good positions means living well, but that is completely wrong. You must become heavenly warriors who build heaven in practical environments. This is the ideology that Unification Church members must hold, and it is the tradition that the history of unification has left behind. Therefore, you must take responsibility for this history. Those who cannot take responsibility for this history and only consume it become rebels in heaven, while those who illuminate this history become loyal subjects in heaven. 
For this reason, knowing the will of the father who hopes for heaven, we have established Parents' Day, Children's Day, and All Things Day in our time today, but we have not been able to find and establish God's Day. We must march and struggle for the day when the laughter of having achieved heaven will resonate throughout the 3,000 ri peninsula and the entire earth. Given our position, can we afford to rest? There is no time to rest. We must go on and live a life where we wake up startled even while sleeping. These are the Unification Church members. You must become Unification Church members who cry and wail even while eating. 
Why must it be this way? It is to fulfill the heaven that God hoped for and to resolve the grievances of Jesus and the Holy Spirit, who could not fulfill their mission, and the countless saints who could not establish the heavenly kingdom on earth due to the process of sacrifice. Only then can they be liberated. 
Knowing this tremendous content and bearing this tremendous mission, where is there time for us to rest? Even if our legs break, even if we die, we must go on the path of restoration with all our strength. 
The teacher has commanded you to walk the three-year course. Anyone who walks this path must be prepared for death. There are many hardships along this path. You must endure countless trials and walk the thousand-mile journey without any travel expenses. Young maidens must endure humiliation from many people, but to achieve the single-minded purpose they have set, they must go without sleep and starve, risking danger. Does the teacher who has unfolded such circumstances have no responsibility? He does. 
Therefore, what the teacher desires is that when you stand in such a position, you do not complain about anyone. Even if you fall and sacrifice in such a position, do not lament. How could there be no arrows from enemies for those who are laying the foundation to build heaven? How could the enemy not surround them? It is possible. However, the heart that seeks to serve the teacher and God is not for oneself, but for this nation and for the world, so that position is a holy one. Even if the path is long, you must know that the footsteps of the warriors of unification are to find the shortcut and go joyfully. 
Today, you must step forward with the ideology of unification, crossing walls and borders, before the 3,000 ri peninsula and the 30 million people. The current situation in Korea requires even the youth on the streets to be educated in the ideology of unification. Such things must happen. Otherwise, you will feel immediately that you are doomed. 
In walking this path, you must possess the heart of a parent and use the body of a servant, shedding tears for humanity, sweat for the earth, and blood for heaven. Only then will the value of your tears, sweat, and blood be recognized by humanity, the earth, and heaven. 
God comes riding on the foundation of sacrifice. He has been working through the personal, familial, tribal, national, and global sacrificial eras. Therefore, today, Unification Church members must go through the personal sacrificial era and fulfill their responsibilities in the national sacrificial era to advance toward the global sacrificial path. 
Thus, you should stand in the lowest position possible. While others go on vacation during the hot summer months, and students all go on break to play, you must go back to your hometown and learn farming, even if it means blistering your hands and feet. You must become farmers. You must become those who pull carts. Thus, Unification Church members must become friends of this nation and patriots of this country. Only then can you gradually stand on the path of providential development. 
While there may be many grievances during the three-year course, you must know that God is with us. The teacher said that after the three-year course, the world would change, and it is happening as he said. The time has come when unimaginable things will be decided by our hands. However, there are some members who are getting tired as they pass through the challenges of the three-year course. You must not look at the tired ones and fear that you too will become tired. Do not tire; you must testify and persevere until the end. 
God is currently fighting a battle with Satan. As God stands at this crossroads and fights, we, who must fulfill the duty of loyalty and filial piety, cannot tire. We are like a bomb. Even if I explode and my body is shattered, I cannot sit down. 
Now we are in the process of going through the four-year course. We must go through the remaining three years cleanly. 
The path of restoration that still needs to be walked 
Around the beginning of October, the district leaders responsible for South Korea were re-elected. Until now, they have only known how to give orders from the position of leaders, without understanding the circumstances of the members. Therefore, they are being told to walk this path again from the position of the members. 
Seeing the district leaders standing on the front line, worrying about God's will and moving toward the world restoration, you too must follow that path. Do you want to follow, or not? "We will follow." 
We have circumstances that we cannot avoid. This path is not one that ministers of this country or those in positions of authority can walk. Only those who can die for heaven can walk this path. When you encounter the poor or the abandoned in your local areas, you must not become a disgraceful group that avoids them. You must have this ideology and conviction in the stage of activity where you live and evangelize them. Doing so will benefit your descendants and will fulfill God's will. 
If we do not do this, our ancestors and descendants will accuse us. 
Because Adam fell, countless descendants have criticized Adam for violating the laws of heaven. Adam and Eve fell because they could not resist the temptation of the archangel, Satan. Therefore, the more chaotic the times and environment become, the stronger and bolder you must be with the conviction to receive God's dominion. You are warriors who have stepped forward to fulfill God's will. 
What does communism mean in this beautiful land? If hundreds of thousands of soldiers are armed with our ideology of unification, communism will collapse in an instant. Therefore, you must recognize how heavy the responsibility of the mission laid upon us today is and the path we must walk. 
History may flow, but our responsibilities cannot flow away. Even if the world rests, we cannot rest. We must establish a day of certain victory and fulfill the heavenly kingdom that God desires. If we do not, we must understand the tremendous fact that we will be accused before our descendants. Therefore, you must become those who struggle for these things. Place your descendants and nation before God, and the world...
You must walk the path, pray, and put in your sincere effort.  
You still have a journey of return ahead of you. In walking the path of return, you must prepare the standards of the previous stage before you can pray for yourself. That is the law of heaven. And as a co-worker of God, dying is the inevitable law of heaven.  
So how should we die? That is the question.  
In the end, we must illuminate heaven, creating a foundation where the nation and the world can follow us and bow their heads before God. Only then can we consider it a success.  
The young men and women of the Unification Church gathered here must walk the path of pioneers who can ignite the fire of God's word in all young people and lead them to God. To do this, you must be strong and courageous. Thus, you still have the path of return to walk.  
Many people around the world are calling us, and we must walk that path. In the process of the next six months, regional leaders and district leaders will feel many hardships in starting a special journey. They will come to understand how difficult the position of a public responsibility holder is.  
Those of you who are active this time must inherit the tradition of the past teachers who directly engaged in the work. I want to risk my life for the nation, but I ask you to act diligently as my representatives. You should recognize that participating in this six-month period is very valuable, and even when you return, you must absolutely obey the words of your leaders. However, you should have a heart of indignation towards the world. That is what is better for you.  
Today, the members across the nation must understand for whom the work of the teacher is being done. And you must be prepared internally and externally to mobilize the whole. Everything depends on you. So even if you find yourselves in difficult circumstances, you must put in your sincere effort for the brothers who have stepped forward for the cause. Do you understand? "Yes."  
Every time you eat and feel full, you should feel ashamed.  
While I eat to my fill, our district leader cannot eat a full bowl of rice. You must be able to reflect on this. Even when you sleep, you should be concerned about how the district leader is sleeping and pray for him. Practicing this kind of life means that there is still a path of return to walk. Unless we achieve victory over the national Golgotha, we cannot head towards the global Golgotha city. Therefore, today we have a path of return to walk towards the global Golgotha and the heavenly Golgotha. Since God's desire is to establish heaven through the path of return, we must continue to walk today and again tomorrow. No matter what circumstances arise, whether parents oppose, siblings oppose, or peers oppose, we must go.  
As long as there is a path of return to walk, we cannot stop. Even if it takes eons, we must go, and even through our descendants for millions of generations, this path must be walked.
